  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a669efa7-c8da-41d1-b794-da42dea5a0c3'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText6241463184223810704" style="display:none">How do you keep going when you feel like your life is over?<br /><br />Maggie never thought she’d see Clay again. So, she attempts to put her life back together after her heart has been shattered to pieces. Moving on and moving forward, just as Clay wanted her to.<br /><br />Clay never stopped thinking of Maggie. Even after ripping their lives apart and leaving her behind to get the help he so desperately needed. He is healing...slowly. But his heart still belongs to the girl who tried to save him.<br /><br />When a sudden tragedy brings Maggie and Clay face to face again, nothing is the same. Yet some things never change. Can the darkness that threatened to consume them be transformed into something else and finally give them what they always wanted? And can two people who fought so hard to be together, finally find their happiness? Or will their demons and fear drive them apart for good?<br /><br />The thing about love, is even when it destroys you, it has a way of mending what is broken. And in the shadows, you can still see the light.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1682809863115492245"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406371i/792703._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406371i/792704.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406371i/792705.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> PHENOMENAL! I was in love with this story from the first word, until the very last. </b><br/><br/><i> "For those searching for the light... Never stop." </i><br/><br/>I can't even tell you how much I needed this book after finishing book #1 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_' title='Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters' rel='nofollow noopener'>Find You in the Dark</a>. FYITD was one of the absolute best books I've ever read and I felt so connected to the characters and drawn into the story that, honestly, my world was just not complete until I was able to read this book.<br/><br/>This book kept me up till 5AM. I just had to read it in one si</span>
  <span id="freeText1682809863115492245" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406371i/792703._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406371i/792704.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406371i/792705.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> PHENOMENAL! I was in love with this story from the first word, until the very last. </b><br><br><i> "For those searching for the light... Never stop." </i><br><br>I can't even tell you how much I needed this book after finishing book #1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_" title="Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">Find You in the Dark</a>. FYITD was one of the absolute best books I've ever read and I felt so connected to the characters and drawn into the story that, honestly, my world was just not complete until I was able to read this book.<br><br>This book kept me up till 5AM. I just had to read it in one sitting, there was no way I was putting this book down!<br><br>The story was a direct continuation of book #1. It focuses a lot on healing, on recovery, on finding a healthy balance to life... on finding the light in the shadows ♥ (sniff... I'm getting teary here)<br><br>I want to take a minute and talk about Clay. I loved how well the author described him. Because despite having a mental condition, he was downright swoony. Everything about him was just pure, gorgeous, normal, rational, hot guy swoon material, he just also had an illness.<br><br>With the way the author described his POV, I felt like I got right inside his head. She wrote him in such a way that I couldn't help but sympathize with everything he went though. I experienced his mood swings with him. I was right there with him every step of the way. He had good days and bad days, days of coming to terms with things, days of gut wrenching pain and days of elation. I felt his highs, I felt his lows, I was totally connected to everything he went through.<br><br><b> <i> "Just when I thought I had things under control, the reality of who I was smacked me squarely in the face. Being nuts was no fun let me tell you... my kind of nuts was scary and consuming... I was a far cry from being the man I wanted to be. But I was getting there." </i> </b><br><br>I think also that the fact that he had this condition made how much he loved Maggie so much stronger. Because he truly did - with every fiber of his being. And the fact that that love he felt was strong enough to make him push through everything was heart warming, inspiring and just downright beautiful.<br><br><i> <b> "For a guy who struggled with finding his place in the world, standing next to Maggie, I understood one thing on a very fundamental level. Wherever she went, whatever she did, that is where I belonged." </b> </i><br><br>Maggie was such a strong heroine. She had her moments of weakness, but the depth of her love for Clay was enough to get her through anything. I loved watching them work together to make things work.<br><br><i> <b> "My love for this beautifully broken, yet slowly healing boy, made me strong.... My soul belonged with him, was so entangled in him that I was no longer a single being." </b> </i><br><br>Clay and Maggie's connection had always been intense to an extreme. Everything about them was heightened. And as a reader, I felt it SO strongly. Regardless of if they were even in the same scene together, sometimes just their feelings for each other would hit me so strongly (in a thought, memory, or note) and I'd just start to tear up.<br><br>The struggle they went though broke my heart. But I loved how strong they both were. I honestly have to say that despite the struggle of what they went through, they were really one of the most functional relationships I've read. To go through what they went through and to be able to come out of it strong and together was downright admirable.<br><br>They were both trying with all their heart, fighting the odds, and proving that love could truly conquer all.<br><br><i> <b> "It was just two people who loved each other, trying to make some sense in a world where there was none." </b></i> <br><br>It was a rough, bumpy road. It was raw. Imperfect. Messy. But my dear God did I love this journey and this story.<br><br>It was no fairy tale, but it was true love that you felt with your whole heart.<br><br>I cried my way through the epilogue and when I finished the book, I literally just sat there with tears pouring down my face for several minutes... just over flowing with emotions ♥♥<br><br>Yes, there is a happy ending. It was believable, real, and absolutely perfect for them. The author truly did these beautiful characters justice.<br><br>Guys, this book duet is just incredible. I highly recommend them if you are in the mood for a beautiful, emotional, and unconventional love story.<br><br>Clay and Maggie's story will remain in my heart forever ♥<br><br><i> <b> "You are everything good in my life. Even when I had thought all I had was the darkness... you gave me something to live for." </b></i> <br><br>CASTING (see above images) and see my review of book #1 for individual casting images: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/473035968">http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/...</a><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406371i/792706._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="1682809863115492245" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer7837572745629048376"><b>5+ I <3 CLAYTON REED STARS!!!</b><br/><br/><b>

</b><br/><br/>Clay and Maggie’s journey continues...<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/65e4c562-b646-4a04-a672-b398f5fc4e3a_zps12fa6e4a.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Find You in the Dark was one of my favorite books of 2012. I fell in love with Clayton Reed... and I loved Maggie too :D I have been waiting and waiting for this book, and it was worth the wait!!! Now, back to Find You in the Dark- The ending was crazy... <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[After Clay’s suicide attempt, Cl</span></span>
  <span id="freeText7837572745629048376" style="display:none"><b>5+ I &lt;3 CLAYTON REED STARS!!!</b><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>The thing about shadows is that they’re not all darkness. You need to have light to have shadows. So just look for it.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Clay and Maggie’s journey continues...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/65e4c562-b646-4a04-a672-b398f5fc4e3a_zps12fa6e4a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401803i/780250._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 65e4c562-b646-4a04-a672-b398f5fc4e3a_zps12fa6e4a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/f75faf53-5fa7-42db-a4bc-a85e32d6a7a7_zpsbd9566cc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Find You in the Dark was one of my favorite books of 2012. I fell in love with Clayton Reed... and I loved Maggie too :D I have been waiting and waiting for this book, and it was worth the wait!!! Now, back to Find You in the Dark- The ending was crazy... <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[After Clay’s suicide attempt, Clay was institutionalized and Maggie was left home, broken. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Light in the Shadows starts off where FYitD left off. Clay is in Florida, trying to better himself and Maggie is at home in Virginia, trying (unsuccessfully) to move on with her life after Clay. She’s depressed, upset, and after receiving a letter from Clay- she gets angry. Clay doesn’t know what to do. He has to focus on himself and getting better. He doesn’t think he’s good for Maggie. He is doing good for himself, making progress. He learns a lot about himself and how to cope. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/83d3814d-2360-4ee1-809c-85f5a73552ed_zpsa28922f8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401803i/780252.jpg" alt=" photo 83d3814d-2360-4ee1-809c-85f5a73552ed_zpsa28922f8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Clay is still in love with Maggie, but he can’t do anything but focus on treatment, and Maggie is still very much in love with Clay, even if she is angry.<br><b>
  <blockquote>I would never move on from Clay. My soul belonged with him, was so entangled in him that I was no longer a single being.</blockquote>
</b><br>After tragedy strikes in Virginia <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Clay’s aunt Ruby’s partner Lisa dies... tears :( <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Clay comes back. He and Maggie see each other for the first time in three months. They are cordial, but try to keep their distance at first. Their attempts are futile. <br><b>
  <blockquote>It was like every time we were together, our bodies orbited around each other as if pulled by an invisible force that we had no control over.</blockquote>
</b>  After much contemplation on both sides, they decide to give it another go. They both know it won’t be easy. There are a lot of unresolved issues, but they both are still very much in love with each other. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Was it possible to go back to the beginning? To try and re-write a history that had already come to define us? To change the direction of fate and see where it took us?</blockquote>
</b>  This time will be different. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/b79cda57-84e2-4098-a080-378915c852e3_zps203d7aea.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401803i/780253.jpg" alt=" photo b79cda57-84e2-4098-a080-378915c852e3_zps203d7aea.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>They have to learn to communicate, Maggie can’t be her old self, and Clay can’t go into his old patterns. It isn’t an easy road for either of them, but they are willing to fight for it. I love being in Clay’s head for half of this book. Seeing his struggle, and him doing the right thing in the end, I was so happy for him, so proud. No matter what happened between him and Maggie, they were willing to figure it out together.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/a31d9ae1-2372-4ac1-8a55-13714a307d27_zps8dc089fb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401803i/780254.jpg" alt=" photo a31d9ae1-2372-4ac1-8a55-13714a307d27_zps8dc089fb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh Clay and Maggie... I love them both so much! Seriously, one of my favorite fictional couples. This book just made me so happy! Clay has his issues, but he is still one of my favorite book boyfriends. He is the sweetest, kindest guy... plus he is down right sexy and swoonworthy! And Maggie... she is strong. The unconditional love these two have is just beautiful. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/73abe03f-da6a-45b3-8234-e1e30e57b322_zpsdcfd4140.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401803i/780255.jpg" alt=" photo 73abe03f-da6a-45b3-8234-e1e30e57b322_zpsdcfd4140.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Such an inspiring and gorgeous story.... I cannot say enough good things about these books! The author is so talented. It is a story with characters I will never forget. I cried so many happy tears, it was just wonderful- the ending and epilogue was perfection. Incredible, phenomenal, fantastic and heartwarming. If you haven’t read these books, you are truly missing out. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/fcc06fec-ea95-48cc-8024-82ea4cf3023a_zps6074dcab.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401803i/780256.jpg" alt=" photo fcc06fec-ea95-48cc-8024-82ea4cf3023a_zps6074dcab.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/486954708?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2013-release">2013-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer486954708" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8562516583091859449"><br/><b>♥ 5+ WONDERFUL, MESMERIZING, EARTH-SHATTERING STARS. ♥</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"The thing about the shadows is that they're not all darkness. You need to have light to have shadows. Just look for it."</i>
</b><br/><br/><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402256ra/781740.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><br/>After how the first part of the series ended I just HAD to know how the story of Maggie and Clay would continue. Therefore, I'm extremely glad that I waited to read this series until the second part was released. Just like the first one, <i>Light in the Shadows</i> made me feel *so many emotions*. It was heartbreaking, sad</span>
  <span id="freeText8562516583091859449" style="display:none"><br><b>♥ 5+ WONDERFUL, MESMERIZING, EARTH-SHATTERING STARS. ♥</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"The thing about the shadows is that they're not all darkness. You need to have light to have shadows. Just look for it."</i>
</b><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402256ra/781740.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br>After how the first part of the series ended I just HAD to know how the story of Maggie and Clay would continue. Therefore, I'm extremely glad that I waited to read this series until the second part was released. Just like the first one, <i>Light in the Shadows</i> made me feel *so many emotions*. It was heartbreaking, sad and some parts were difficult to read but after all, all the emotions were so worth it... This series really managed to hold my attention from the first moment I started reading it and after a while it became a HUGE page-turner for me, and I was constantly anxious to find out what would happen next. <br><br><br>At the end of <i>Find You in the Dark</i> Maggie made herself a promise:<br><br><b>
  <i>"Because I was Maggie Young. And from now on I vowed to stay out of the dark."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397390i/766764.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After her entire world has been shattered to pieces, she tries to move on and not let her past with Clay consume her. But, deep down, she knows she might never be able to get over someone like him. For Clay himself, the dark still loomed around the corner as well...<br><br>It all starts out with a heartbreaking and beautiful prologue.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Forgive. <br><br>Such a small word. Only seven letters but they carried the weight of the world.<br><br>Seven letters between me and the one thing I wanted most in my life.<br><br>No word in the history of words was harder to give and even more difficult to receive.<br><br>But I needed it. Craved my redemption deep in my bones.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Clay is determined to work on <u>himself</u> first in order to become the kind of person, Maggie deserves. While trying to control his issues with the much needed help of professionals, Clay slowly but surely learns how to find the light within the darkness of his shadows. <br><br>The journey of Maggie and Clay is not an easy one. It's an extremely emotional ride with a lot of ups and downs but still, I enjoyed every second of it. Because it was real, truthful and it was <u>their</u> journey. Clay and Maggie are such complex, yet highly endearing characters. Especially Clay's way of thinking, isn't always easy to relate to, but in the end, I perfectly understood why he acted the way he did and all I can say is that I LOVE him for it. And reading his POV, only made me understand where's coming from even better.<br><br>Together with the help from the people who truly care about him (unlike his coldhearted and awful parents, who I truly despised!), Clay learns that the darkness doesn't have to be all-consuming. You just have to fight for it and remember that there's always light at the end of the tunnel.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You are everything good in my life. Even when I thought all I had was the darkness, you were there. And you gave ma something to live for. I couldn't let you go. No matter how hard I tried. I know now that's because to lose you would be losing the very best part of myself."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402256i/781741.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>"Over six years ago I met a girl who saved me. I didn't realize at the time, mostly because her attitude pissed me off, that she would become the most important thing in my life. <br><br>But then I got to know her and when I was drowning, she became my air. In the cold, she became my warmth.<br><br>In the dark, she became my light."</i> ~ Clay &lt;3 <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397390i/766765.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Find You in the Dark</b> is one of the best series I've ever read and I would highly recommend everyone to embark on this beautiful and unforgettable journey with Maggie and Clay, and hopefully you'll fall in love with them just as much as I did.<br><br>~~~<br><br>♥ <b>
  <i>"There is more beauty inside you than in anyone I ever met."</i>
</b> ♥<br></span>

<div id="review_487356309" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/487356309" />
    <a title="Annie Brewer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer"><img alt="Annie Brewer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442496062p2/5315988.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/487356309?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie Brewer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie Brewer" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer">Annie Brewer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=depressing-dark-mental-health-issue">depressing-dark-mental-health-issue</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=male-point-of-view">male-point-of-view</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=tearjerker">tearjerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=2013-must-have">2013-must-have</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=5-star-worthy">5-star-worthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=books-i-want-now">books-i-want-now</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=favorite-hotties">favorite-hotties</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer487356309" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14785685083488176006">FIRST OF ALL, THANK YOU WALTERS AND KIM FOR AN ARC!!!! <br/><br/>5 UNBELIEVABLE*FANTASTIC*SUPERB*EMOTIONAL*BITTERSWEET*PHENOMENAL* STARS!!!!!!<br/><br/>Okay, well I've put off writing my review long enough. It seems when it comes to this series, my emotions will never be the same. These books are just too incredible for words, it's hard to think about them without shedding so many tears. Tears of joy for the outcome of this beautiful story. Tears of heartache for all these beautiful characters had to endure. Tears </span>
  <span id="freeText14785685083488176006" style="display:none">FIRST OF ALL, THANK YOU WALTERS AND KIM FOR AN ARC!!!! <br><br>5 UNBELIEVABLE*FANTASTIC*SUPERB*EMOTIONAL*BITTERSWEET*PHENOMENAL* STARS!!!!!!<br><br>Okay, well I've put off writing my review long enough. It seems when it comes to this series, my emotions will never be the same. These books are just too incredible for words, it's hard to think about them without shedding so many tears. Tears of joy for the outcome of this beautiful story. Tears of heartache for all these beautiful characters had to endure. Tears of sadness for the very fact that this series is over, no more Clay and Maggie. Oh how I'll miss them so much. So. Damn. Much. <br><br>I loved Find You in the Dark. Like LOVED it. I raved about it. I knew it was dark and disturbing when I picked it up. I knew it wouldn't be a fluff or fairy tale kind of story. But as I started it, I was so immersed in the story I didn't care. Clay was such a sick boy, he needed to be saved. And Maggie comes along and falls for him just as the rest of us had. He was mentally sick, yes. But underneath the illness and unstable behavior, he was just a boy trying to fit into the world. His parents didn't show him love, they were ashamed of him because of his illness. Let me talk about that for a minute....<br><br>What the fuck kind of parent tells their only child that they're an embarrassment and should be locked away so it doesn't have an effect on how THEY look to the public?? OH MY FUCKING GOD! It's no wonder Clay was ashamed of himself and so fucked up. He had no support from the people who are supposed to love him unconditionally. They made him feel like he was worthless, a fuck up. Well, let me tell you....he was far from a fuck up because in my eyes, he was strong and perfect. It wasn't his fault that he sick. Fucking A those assholes wanted to send him away so they wouldn't have to deal with their son's mental instability. GAH, I'm furious. Just thinking about them makes me want to vomit and then gauge their eyes out.<br><br>That said, I won't go into FYitD because if you've read it, you know what happens. I don't have to go into that....though, I will say this book picks up where FYitD left off. Yes, there was a cliffhanger and I was DYING, DYING for the next one. And thanks to Walters and Kim for sending me an ARC of this amazing conclusion. I was so thrilled to get my hands on this gem. It was like a dream come true. I got into it right away and was again, immersed into the whirlwind rollercoaster of Clay and Maggie. It was worth every heartache and tear I shed, and believe me, I shed A LOT of tears. This book met every expectation I had and then some.<br><br>The prologue. Oh god, that prologue had me in tears. It was amazing.<br><br>"Forgive. Such a small word. Only seven letters but they carried the weight of the world. Seven letters between me and the one thing I wanted most in my life."<br><br>*wipes tears*<br><br>So Clay is in Florida at the Center getting help. He's been there for almost 3 months. And almost 3 months ago he tried to end his life. Maggie saved him but she had to let him go. He needed more help than she could give him. So now she's at home in Virginia trying to pick up the pieces of her crazy life and move on.<br><br>Only one problem....she can't. She loves the only boy who made her life worth living. He showed her how to live, even though he was so sick. When they were together and doing good, they were REALLY GOOD. But things took a turn quickly and it started to become too much for her. After all, she's only 17. How does one handle such a monumental circumstance? She did the best she could and she loved this boy with all her heart and soul, which is why she had to set him free. But she's struggling to let go completely. Deep down she knows they belong together.<br><br>"My love for this beautifully broken, yet slowly healing boy, made me strong.... My soul belonged with him, was so entangled in him that I was no longer a single being." -Maggie Mae Young<br><br>Tragedy strikes, sending Clay back to Davidson for a funeral. Ah, my heart. My heart was crying for these people. Clay. Ruby. Lisa. So sad.<br><br>Clay and Maggie see each other. <br><br>"It was like every time we were together. Our bodies orbited around each other as if pulled by an invisible force that we had no control over. I wanted this. And I wanted to run from it. I wanted to pull her in and never let go. And I wanted to push her away."-Clay<br><br>"Seeing him again had only confirmed what my subconscious already knew. I would never move on from Clay. My soul belonged with him, was so entangled in him that I was no longer a single being." -Maggie<br><br>The two of them, together again, it was like nothing had changed. Yet everything had changed. But it was beautiful and heartbreaking. Real and hopeful. The whole time, I kept thinking, they have to be together. They have to be. But how are they going to make it work? I had so many fears for them. I was nervous, happy, scared and overjoyed at their reunion. The circumstance which brought them back together was so hard to see. I cried the whole time. Clay had suffered so much yet more shit piled on top and I was so scared he'd relapse. But god, he was so strong compared to FYitD. I was so proud of him. Not to mention, he had a great support...Dr Todd was fantastic in helping with his progress. <br><br>"There’s nothing weak in acknowledging when things are greater than you.” -Dr Todd<br><br>There were times he'd have a panic attack and had to calm himself, fight his demons because he so badly wanted to give in and give up, and cut himself so he wouldn't feel the pain anymore. But with the steps he remembered from treatment, he overcame the urge to give in. I was sooooo proud of him. His struggles were so real and heartbreaking. I felt everything he went through. I loved that we got his POV. Thank you Walters for writing it that way. I don't think I would have felt his heartache and emotions so clearly if we didn't have his POV, and to be honest, I wouldn't have felt so connected to him either. I actually don't think it would have worked at all without it. Some books are mandatory for both MC's POV and this was one of them. I cried when he cried, I felt happiness when he did, I felt his fears, sorrow, guilt, love, loss and grief so deeply that I couldn't concentrate on anything else while I was reading it. This book both shattered my heart yet healed my soul. <br><br>I loved Daniel and Rachel so much in this book. At first they pissed me off when they kept urging Maggie to move on and get over Clay. I wanted to punch them in the face a few times. But I also understood they were just looking out for their best friend. They saw what she went through the first time. Hell, they went through it with her. I admire them for being such amazing best friends. But once things with Clay and Maggie started up again, they backed off. And then....Daniel made me cry.<br><br>“Look, man. I know I haven’t been the most… uh… supportive of you and Maggie. And I’m still not sure how I feel seeing the two of you all up in each other’s asses again. But, I know you’re a decent guy. So for now, I’m reserving judgment." <br>“Okay, so that sounded way assier than I meant it to. What I’m trying to say, is I know you’re dealing with shit. A lot of shit by the looks of it. And for Maggie’s sake… well… and yours too, I won’t be the speed bump on your road to the candy castle or whatever.” -Daniel Lowe<br><br>He really tried to be friends and give Clay the benefit of the doubt. I loved him for that. It made my heart happy to see them getting along. Things between Maggie and Clay couldn't have been more rockier or intense. But when they were together, it was the most beautiful thing I'd ever seen. Maggie was so supportive and the fact that she agreed to go to therapy with Clay just made me cry with happiness for them. They wanted to really make it work this time. Clay went to great lengths to change and be the man he felt she deserved. Maggie went to great lengths to show the boy she loved with everything she has that she would support him no matter what. And she really grew in this one. She didn't stand down when he occasionally lashed out at her or cower to him. She stood up and made him see she wasn't going anywhere this time. It was just...perfect. Beautiful. God, I love them so much. These two endured so much yet they overcame it and came out stronger in the end. My heart is so full of emotion when I think about these books. Walters portrayed such a tough subject so real and raw, you could feel the realism in your bones. It was as if you were experiencing it yourself, which in a way you were. Walters has an amazing gift. <br><br>I'll never forget this story as long as I live. Clay and Maggie will FOREVER live in my heart and I will take them with me to my grave and never forget them. I love them so much. I cried for over 30 minutes when I finished reading this book. I was glad to have read it and experience it, but was so sad to say goodbye to my favorite fictional couple.<br><br>The ending. Oh god, that ending had me in a weepy mess. So amazing and wonderful and bittersweet. Oh Clay, how I love the fuck out of you.<br><br><br><br>“Over six years ago I met a girl who saved me. I didn't realize at the time, mostly because her attitude pissed me off, that she would become the most important thing in my life. But then I got to know her and when I was drowning, she became my air. In the cold, she became my warmth. In the dark, she became my light,”-Clayton Reed<br><br>Oh Clay, I'll never, ever forget you. You've ruined all other fictional boys for me. You'll forever be in my heart and I'll love you for all eternity. *wipes tears*<br><br>"For a guy who struggled with finding his place in the world, standing next to Maggie, I understood one thing on a very fundamental level. Wherever she went, whatever she did, that is where I belonged." <br><br>If you haven't read these books, you really need to. These books are phenomenal and it shows that love is above all the most important thing in life. Thank you Walters for writing such an extraordinary series that will forever live in my heart. <br><br>I got to interview Mrs. Walters so it will be on my blog for the blog tour. <br><br><br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/Review%20Pics/Find%20you%20in%20the%20dark/FYITD_zps21a16fd5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402312i/781869.jpg" alt=" photo FYITD_zps21a16fd5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>PLEASE.<br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/Find%20You%20in%20the%20Dark/pray_zps2492b20d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402312i/781870.jpg" alt=" photo pray_zps2492b20d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/Find%20You%20in%20the%20Dark/love3_zps2c980db9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380365501i/717598.jpg" alt=" photo love3_zps2c980db9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/Find%20You%20in%20the%20Dark/LOVE_zps407b7207.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402312i/781871.png" alt=" photo LOVE_zps407b7207.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>CLAY &amp; MAGGIE<br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/Find%20You%20in%20the%20Dark/maggieandclay_zps0671c47d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/Find%20You%20in%20the%20Dark/love_zps50b93f27.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402312i/781873.jpg" alt=" photo love_zps50b93f27.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/Find%20You%20in%20the%20Dark/love1_zps5f73bf80.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402312i/781874.jpg" alt=" photo love1_zps5f73bf80.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/Find%20You%20in%20the%20Dark/love2_zps04619f1f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402312i/781875.jpg" alt=" photo love2_zps04619f1f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I LOVE CLAYTON REED!!!!!<br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/Find%20You%20in%20the%20Dark/clay_zpsb63cc729.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402312ra/781876.gif" alt=" photo clay_zpsb63cc729.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Update: <br><br>LOVE LOVE LOVE LOVE LOVE LOVE LOVE LOVE LOVE LOVE!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! I want CLAY! I WANT CLAY FUCKING REED! Ahhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhh!!!! <br><br>Review to come after release! But to everyone worried, don't be...just have lots of tissues handy and enjoy the emotional rollercoaster ride. It is every bit worth the heartache. I'm at a loss for words and this exceeded my expectations. I love Clay. I love him so damn much!!!!!! I can't wait for you all to read it! Now I must go finish crying because this book took so much out of me and I'm not done being emotional.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer589980953" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8789337294606011141"><b>5 LUMINOUS Stars<br/><br/><i>"When I was drowning, she became my air. In the cold, she became my warmth. In the dark, she became my light.”</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393705ra/758056.gif' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Darkness' true meaning is the absence of light. But it takes both for stars to shine, for shadows to comfort you, cloud your mind and relieve the burden in your soul. Light and darkness, forever entwined. Healing and loving, scabbing over wounds and mending the pieces of broken hearts.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417579ra/826110.gif' width='400' height='650' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Picking up, where <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_' title='Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters' rel='nofollow noopener'>Find You in the Dark</a> left us almost "dead", this second book in the ri</span>
  <span id="freeText8789337294606011141" style="display:none"><b>5 LUMINOUS Stars<br><br><i>"When I was drowning, she became my air. In the cold, she became my warmth. In the dark, she became my light.”</i></b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393705ra/758056.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Darkness' true meaning is the absence of light. But it takes both for stars to shine, for shadows to comfort you, cloud your mind and relieve the burden in your soul. Light and darkness, forever entwined. Healing and loving, scabbing over wounds and mending the pieces of broken hearts.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417579ra/826110.gif" width="400" height="650" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Picking up, where <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_" title="Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">Find You in the Dark</a> left us almost "dead", this second book in the riveting and emotional series by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5416410.A__Meredith_Walters" title="A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">A. Meredith Walters</a>, again manages to enthrall and fascinate.<br><br>In alternate POVs, Clay and Maggie share their story. These two kids will fight heaven and hell for their much deserved happily ever after, coming to realise that sometimes, when you can't banish the darkness completely, just light a candle and hope to find the other half of your damaged soul, waiting for you.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417579ra/826111.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the end of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_" title="Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">Find You in the Dark</a>, Clay made the ultimate sacrifice. He set Maggie free. To love again, to have a life.<br><br>He tries to heal and find the courage to move on and become whole. To earn a second chance at living.<br><br><b>
  <i>"You can make this work for you. And when you feel like you can’t do it, that’s when you need to ask for help. Never be ashamed to admit you can’t handle it. There’s nothing weak in acknowledging when things are greater than you.”</i>
</b><br><br>He feels inadequate and undeserving of love, happiness and his Maggie.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417579i/826112.jpg" width="400" height="297" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A tragedy will summon him back to place he left his heart and give him the opportunity to see his mistakes and move past them. But above all to prove himself to Maggie. His salvation and his trigger, hoping she will want him back. <br><br><b>
  <i>“You are everything good in my life. Even when I thought all I had was the darkness, you were there.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417579ra/826113.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maggie was left alone and she can't forget. She tries to move on but there is no life and happiness without Clay. Can she trust him? Or are they doomed to make the same mistakes, all over again?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/457822.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Will they have a future? Or just a few precious moments of sanity, until once again the dreaded, all-consuming darkness descends upon them?<br><br><b>
  <i>“Pour toute ma vie, de tout mon coeur.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411131i/806994._SX540_.png" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>As I have already mentioned in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/454269005" rel="nofollow noopener">my review</a> of the first book, this story handles a very serious and real issue, with care, dignity and tenderness. It evokes all your feelings and it speaks directly to your heart. You root and cheer for love. And you pray that it will prove enough.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417579i/826114.jpg" width="400" height="232" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A highly recommended series in the young adult genre. But truly YA is just a label. Don't let it bother you. Clay and Maggie are above such things...<br><br><b>Read these books and I'm sure you won't regret it! </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417579i/826115._SX540_.jpg" width="500" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>This review can be found on my blog: <a href="http://infinity-of-time.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">infinity-of-time.blogspot.com</a> also known as... </i>
</b><br><a href="http://infinity-of-time.blogspot.gr/2013/04/light-in-shadows-find-you-in-dark-2-by_21.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380363317i/714576.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

<div id="review_522525155" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/522525155" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/522525155?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=need-it-in-paperback">need-it-in-paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=college-romance">college-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=got-it-in-paperback">got-it-in-paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=angst-filled-reads">angst-filled-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=emotional-reads">emotional-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=ya-reads">ya-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=super-romantic-reads">super-romantic-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=mental-health">mental-health</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer522525155" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4083764847875162783"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407561i/796159._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407561i/796160._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Noooo!!!! <br/><br/>No, there was no cliffhanger, I just sooo did not want this series to end.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I love you, Maggie May Young. Always and forever." And then my mouth touched hers and I felt my future begin.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I stumbled upon Find You in the Dark by chance when I saw someone else's review, and never expected it to pack such a punch. I didn't realise that the first book had a cliffhanger when I went into it, and I remember being so completely floored by it.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Our heads have a nasty habit of rui</b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText4083764847875162783" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407561i/796159._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407561i/796160._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Noooo!!!! <br><br>No, there was no cliffhanger, I just sooo did not want this series to end.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I love you, Maggie May Young. Always and forever." And then my mouth touched hers and I felt my future begin.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I stumbled upon Find You in the Dark by chance when I saw someone else's review, and never expected it to pack such a punch. I didn't realise that the first book had a cliffhanger when I went into it, and I remember being so completely floored by it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Our heads have a nasty habit of ruining what can make us happiest. And there are times in our lives when you have to put aside what we think is best and do with what you feel is best."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And now I've read the second book. I got the HEA I wanted for Maggie and Clay and I'm left feeling a little bereft.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407561i/796161.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love Clay, so so so much. He is probably one of the most complex, tortured characters I have ever read, but he has had such a profound effect on me. This is the type of book that opens up your mind and your heart. I cried for Maggie and Clay, I laughed with them and I lived every second right along side them.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You are everything good in my life. Even when I thought all I had was the darkness, you were there. And you gave me something to live for. I couldn't let you go. No matter how hard I tried. I know now that's because to lose you would be losing the very best part of myself."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The writing is freakin' awesome. There are some priceless one liners that will made me snort my cuppa' tea through my nose. A. Meredith Walters has quite the sense of humour. The writing is candid and perfectly fitting for the age and gender of each character. I loved reading Clay's POV through his therapy, and Maggie is just perfect as a heroine throughout. She is likeable, realistic and ordinary. Gosh, the strength of character she has to show in some part of this story are totally humbling. <br><br>Knowing the author's personal experience with counselling children and teens with mental health issues just makes the story that much more intense. It gives the reading weight and authenticity and made my empathy for the characters just that much rawer. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>There were times I left my sessions feeling like I was a step closer to being the person I wanted to be. The guy who would be able to show up on Maggie May Young's doorstep and tell her that his life would always begin and end with her.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I'd love another novella about Rachel and Daniel, Maggie's two best friends, who's book, 'Cloud Walking', was a great addition to this series, and maybe even something a little extra about Maggie and Clay. Fingers tightly crossed that we hear more from these fabulous characters.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407561i/796162._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you haven't read this yet, or you've been hanging on for the happy ending, don't wait any longer. It's simply superb!<br><br>Don't miss the amazing giveaway for one eCopy of <i>Light in the Shadows</i> right now over on my blog. <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407561i/796163._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Smittens-Book-Blog/525405204177978">http://www.facebook.com/pages/Smitten...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4083764847875162783" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer5832557674266910023"><b>Thank you</b> to everyone who showed their love and support for me after I finished <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/462231313' rel='nofollow noopener'>Find You in the Dark.</a> I love you all and I feel blessed to have bonded with everyone over books. <br/><br/>After my personal heartbreak, at the end of the book one, I knew I had to finish this series. My driving force was<b> I needed Clay to have the HEA my friend, Bill, never got. </b> <br/> <br/>Clay and Maggie's persevered through the darkness to find little glimpses of <b>light in the shadows.</b> Even though they stayed together their lives will</span>
  <span id="freeText5832557674266910023" style="display:none"><b>Thank you</b> to everyone who showed their love and support for me after I finished <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/462231313" rel="nofollow noopener">Find You in the Dark.</a> I love you all and I feel blessed to have bonded with everyone over books. <br><br>After my personal heartbreak, at the end of the book one, I knew I had to finish this series. My driving force was<b> I needed Clay to have the HEA my friend, Bill, never got. </b> <br> <br>Clay and Maggie's persevered through the darkness to find little glimpses of <b>light in the shadows.</b> Even though they stayed together their lives will never be a bed of roses<b> but </b>instead one full of hope and determination. <br><br>This two-part series is a realistic fiction about a beautiful love story with a person who has a mental illness. <b>Light in the Shadows</b> is the healing process Clay and Maggie go through as they learn to manage the mental illness that is part of their relationship. <br><br>Just remember there is light at the end of the tunnel. <br><br>SERIES:<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_" title="Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17155039.Light_in_the_Shadows__Find_You_in_the_Dark___2_" title="Light in the Shadows (Find You in the Dark, #2) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1359612980s/17155039.jpg" alt="Light in the Shadows (Find You in the Dark, #2) by A. Meredith Walters" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br>Continuing story<br><br>Novellas:<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16163857.Cloud_Walking__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_5_" title="Cloud Walking (Find You in the Dark, #1.5) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1357550690s/16163857.jpg" alt="Cloud Walking (Find You in the Dark, #1.5) by A. Meredith Walters" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

One slice and you’ll feel better</i><br/><br/> <b> Maggie Young </b><br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=36l29' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><br/><br/> <b>Clayton Reed</b><br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=33248p2' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410310i/804374.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>

  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410310i/804375.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>This series blew my mind, broke my heart, made me smile, cry, and laugh. I was honored to read the heartbreaking journey of <b> Clay and Maggie </b>, this wasn't simply just a book! millions of teenagers are going through what Clay has been going through everyday and Depression, suicide and cutt</span>
  <span id="freeText6977500291700456422" style="display:none"><b> * 5 EARTH SHATTERING STARS* </b> <br>Lets start this by saying you can't read this without reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754-find-you-in-the-dark" rel="nofollow noopener">Find You In The Dark</a>.<br><br><br><i>Just cut it all away. One slice and you’ll feel better</i><br><br> <b> Maggie Young </b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=36l29" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410310i/804372._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2yzmrzm" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410310i/804373._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br> <b>Clayton Reed</b><br><br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=33248p2" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410310i/804374.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2m7wy6u" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410310i/804375.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>This series blew my mind, broke my heart, made me smile, cry, and laugh. I was honored to read the heartbreaking journey of <b> Clay and Maggie </b>, this wasn't simply just a book! millions of teenagers are going through what Clay has been going through everyday and Depression, suicide and cutting are serious issues they are not to be taken slightly.<br><br><br>I loved reading Clay's point of view, it made me even more heartbroken. i was inside his head i was going through every thing he was. i was feeling the same things, so that made everything intense! <br><br><i>You’d be better off dead.</i><br><br> <br>After everything that happened in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754-find-you-in-the-dark%20" rel="nofollow noopener">Find You in the Dark</a> i needed <b>hope</b> i needed to have my happily ever after through Clay, because i'm feeling him, so on some level i understand him. So for me especially it was very tough for me to read this series, because i felt VERY emotionally connected to the characters. <br><br>This is for sure one of my Favorite books ever! i fell in love with everything in it, the message that this book is presenting is amazing.<br><br><b> <i>“For those searching for the light… Never stop.” </i></b> <br><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZEXWM9msZxY" rel="nofollow noopener">OneRepublic - Mercy </a> This song is very fitting.<br><br>I took several days to finish this, because i wanted to Extend this reading as much as i could, i guess i wasn't prepare to say goodbye to the characters yet.<br><br>this books was a roller coaster! everybody's emotions were all over the place- mine included <br><br>the suffering that Clay went through, i just wanted to jump in the book and hug him and make it okay :(<br><br><b> <i>“Just when I thought I had things under control, the reality of who I was smacked me squarely in the face. Being nuts was no fun let me tell you… my kind of nuts was scary and consuming… I was a far cry from being the man I wanted to be. But I was getting there.” </i></b> <br><br>And at the end as Clay believed Maggie's love did saved him.<br><br><b> <i>“My love for this beautifully broken, yet slowly healing boy, made me strong…. My soul belonged with him, was so entangled in him that I was no longer a single being.”</i></b> <br><br><b> <i>“It was just two people who loved each other, trying to make some sense in a world where there was none.” </i></b> <br><br><br>And the Epilogue was beautiful, and i wanted more! i guess i'll always want more when this guy is concerned. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[“What is this?” she whispered, her eyes never straying from the new artwork. “Did you paint it?” she asked, looking at me over her shoulder.<br>I nodded, letting her take the time to absorb what I was trying to tell her through my picture. It was a silhouette of the two of us, darkened in shadow but with a brilliant, bright light behind us revealing the intricate details of our faces bowed in close together. Butterflies rose in flight around us and it vibrated with the love I felt for the girl standing before it.<br>On the bottom, in neat script, I had carefully written: And he asked her to share his forever.<br>While she stared at the picture, I pulled out the small velvet box I had kept in my pocket all day and got down on one knee. When Maggie turned around and saw what I was doing she gasped, her hands flying to her mouth. And then she did the craziest thing. She fell down to her knees in front of me.<br>“I’m the one who’s supposed to be on my knees here. You’re ruining the moment,” I teased her. She held her hands to my cheeks and gave me one of her earth shattering smiles. It was a smile that could cure cancer. It told me that I was responsible for this perfect slice of happiness in her life.<br>With tears rolling down her face, I tried to tell her with words that could express everything I felt for her, everything she was to me. But words could never be enough to explain the way she had completely filled me.<br>“Over six years ago I met a girl who saved me. I didn’t realize at the time, mostly because her attitude pissed me off, that she would become the most important thing in my life.” Maggie playfully punched my shoulder as I wiped the wetness from her cheeks with my thumbs.<br>“But then I got to know her and when I was drowning, she became my air. In the cold, she became my warmth.” I cupped her face in my hands as she quietly sobbed and for once I didn’t feel any guilt for her tears. Because these tears were filled with nothing but joy. And those were tears I was glad to give her.<br>“In the dark, she became my light,” I whispered, my voice breaking and my own tears started to make their way down my skin.<br>“Our road hasn’t been an easy one. But good things rarely are. You taught me that the person I am is worth loving, worth fighting for. You gave me strength when I had none. You held me up when I wanted to fall. And now, I want to give you everything. I want to give you the world. Because, Maggie, you’ve given me mine. And it’s you. It will always, forever, be you,” I said, the lump in my throat making my voice a harsh whisper.<br>“Clay,” Maggie sobbed and she fell against me, pressing her forehead into my shoulder.<br>Holding her tight against my body, I whispered in her ear, “Will you marry me, Maggie?” She tilted her face up and her smile was absolutely radiant.<br>“I think you already know the answer to that,” she quipped as I slid the diamond ring on her finger, over top the promise ring I had given her all those years ago. Even in the middle of this intense, emotion filled moment, her sarcasm was ever present. And I loved that about her. I kissed every inch of her face, over and over again. “And just so you know, I already have the world. You’re just expanding my universe a little bit,” Maggie added, touching the side of my face and I captured her mouth, kissing her with every ounce of love and adoration I felt for her.<br>And I held her, this girl who had saved me and continued to save me every day. Our path would never be smooth but I hadn’t lied when I said good things were never easy. And I was okay with going the hard way. Because as long as she was beside me, as long as we were together, I knew we could face anything.<br>So together we walked into our future. One that we had mapped out. And that future was nothing but light." <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> &lt;&lt; Parts of the Epilogue<br>Six years later, Clays POV. <br><br><br><br><b> <i> There is more beauty inside you than in anyone I have ever met. These pictures don’t lie. I won’t ever forget you. Or stop loving you. You can ask me to. You can tell me to move on. But I won’t. And I never will. Just don’t forget how beautiful we were. How beautiful we can still be. Please.<br> <br>-Maggie </i></b> <br><br> <br><br><b> <u>Healing,endurance. And most of all courage </u></b> <br>^^^ that what Maggie offered him, and they were the most important things that he needed. she provided that for him. And this is why i loved Maggie. she's such a strong heroine. It's very rare for me to love a heroine in a book , but i absolutely loved her.<br><br><br><b> Depression, suicide and cutting are serious issues.<br>Self-injurious behaviors is often a way for people to cope with bigger issues.<br>If you or someone you know is dealing with cutting or depression, it important to talk about, to get help and find a way to stop!<br>There are so many great resources out there, taking the first step and reaching out is the place to start.</b><br><br><br><b> Depression and bi-polar Support Alliance (DBSA)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.dbsalliance.org">www.dbsalliance.org</a><br> <br><i>Teen Self Injury hotline </i> <br>1-800-Don’t Cut<br> <br><i>Teen Suicide Hotline </i><br>1-800-SUICIDE<br> <br><i>Great resource and information about self-injury </i><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.selfinjury.com">www.selfinjury.com</a> </b><br><br><br><b> Make sure to follow my reviews </b> <br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer583669553" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1185370343073536806"><b>Final rating: 5/5 stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"The thing about the shadows is that they're not all darkness. You need to have light to have shadows. So just look for it” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>One word to say about this series: Wonderful. And to add more words: heartbreaking, powerful, lovely, cute, dark, fascinating, feelings crusher, and so much more. And <i> Light in the shadows </i> is a fascinating and beautiful sequel to <i> Find you in the Dark.</i> And it's definitely one of my favorites now.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"“You are everything good in my lif</b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText1185370343073536806" style="display:none"><b>Final rating: 5/5 stars</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"The thing about the shadows is that they're not all darkness. You need to have light to have shadows. So just look for it” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>One word to say about this series: Wonderful. And to add more words: heartbreaking, powerful, lovely, cute, dark, fascinating, feelings crusher, and so much more. And <i> Light in the shadows </i> is a fascinating and beautiful sequel to <i> Find you in the Dark.</i> And it's definitely one of my favorites now.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"“You are everything good in my life. Even when I thought all I had was the darkness, you were there. And you gave me something to live for. I couldn’t let you go. No matter how hard I tried. I know now that’s because to lose you would be losing the very best part of myself.” I opened my eyes to see Clay staring back at me, tears sliding down his face. He leaned in and his lips a whisper as they closed in.<br> “I love you, Maggie. More than you could ever possibly understand.” "</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And i am sad that the journey of Maggie and Clay is over... Because it will never be over for me... And the ending of this book was so beautiful.... <br><br>This is a story of redemption, of bravery and of love... <br><br><b>[insert dramatic music]</b><br><br><b>And the life gives us a question...would you live with someone who is mentally unstable? Would you love a person who suffers from it? Even if that person is someone you fell in love with? </b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“It the rune Uruz. It’s for healing, endurance, courage. I found it in one of the books Ruby gave me a few weeks back. It just, I don’t know, made sense. I like what it stands for.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>CHARACTERS</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Maggie:</u>
  </i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “I don’t want to wake up ten years from now regretting that I let this slip through my fingers. I don’t want to waste another moment without you in my life"</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Maggie struggles to do what is right for her life... She can't stop loving Clay and she can't move on, even when he told her to do it. She knows he is lying, and she believes it, but then again, she starts to doubt it. She was always there for him, always and forever, she was and is his ever living support, his life, his happiness, every part of his being. And she can't stop loving him, no matter what happens. She is so brave, so wonderful, that even i can't help but love Maggie. <br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Clay:</u>
  </i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"For a guy who struggled with finding his place in the world, standing next to Maggie, I understood one thing on a very fundamental level. Wherever she went, whatever she did, that is where I belonged."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Clay...So broken, so destroyed, but he is slowly recovering and healing... He looked beyond what he saw, he saw that maybe, just a little maybe, there is a possibility for him to have a normal life... Maggie is his life...and he really depends on her. She had shown him that in every darkness there is light... And now she has become his light. And because of her, he wants to <i> change</i>.<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>OTHER CHARACTERS:</u>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Clay's parents =&gt; The worst people i have ever read about...<br>Rachel &amp; Daniel =&gt; cuteness.<br>Ruby &amp; Lisa =&gt; oh my god...beautiful and wonderful people...<br>Maria &amp; Jake =&gt; shoo shoo shooooooooo!!!! ( i don't need you two around)<br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>OVERALL</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br> I cannot describe how much i love this series...Story about Maggie and Clay ended, but i won't forget about them... But i am really really sad that there won't be more :( <br><br>Fantastic work Meredith Walters. You are amazing!<br><br>____________________________________________<br><br>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●<br>____________________________________________ <br><br><b>REVIEW(S) RELATED TO THIS BOOK:</b><br><br>◈ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/583669536" rel="nofollow noopener"> Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) </a> <br>◈ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/583669544" rel="nofollow noopener"> Cloud Walking (Find You in the Dark, #1.5) </a> <br>◈ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/583669553" rel="nofollow noopener"> Light in the Shadows (Find You in the Dark, #2) </a> <br><br><b>
  <i>This review can be found on my blog: <a href="http://infinity-of-time.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">infinity-of-time.blogspot.com</a> also known as... </i>
