<div id="review_480510904" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/480510904" />
    <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag"><img alt="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410910791p2/8191340.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/480510904?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag">Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=ya-na">ya-na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=waiting">waiting</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer480510904" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6351430346696015671"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401293i/778738._SY540_.jpg' width='300' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>"Healing and endurance. And most of all courage. I finally felt, after all this time, that I was mastering these qualities."</b>
</blockquote><br/>When I read and reviewed FYITD, this is part of what I wrote:<br/><i>This heartbreakingly real and gut-wrenching portrayal of a young man suffering crippling mental illness and his journey of survival through the love and salvation of a young woman totally gutted me; I fell completely and deeply in pain and in love with Clay and Maggie.</i> <br/><br/>I thought about their story for a long ti</span>
  <span id="freeText6351430346696015671" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401293i/778738._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Healing and endurance. And most of all courage. I finally felt, after all this time, that I was mastering these qualities."</b>
</blockquote><br>When I read and reviewed FYITD, this is part of what I wrote:<br><i>This heartbreakingly real and gut-wrenching portrayal of a young man suffering crippling mental illness and his journey of survival through the love and salvation of a young woman totally gutted me; I fell completely and deeply in pain and in love with Clay and Maggie.</i> <br><br>I thought about their story for a long time and when the sequel was written, I could not wait to get my hands on it. I had to know how this story would continue and ultimately end. I could not be more pleased with the way the author wrote Light in the Shadows.<br><br>Where FYITD was a fast-paced frenzied emotional roller coaster of the highest highs and the lowest of all lows, LITS was a slow long road to recovery. I fell in love all over again with <b>“this beautifully broken, yet slowly healing boy.”</b> <br><br>Yes, there were tears-many tears and also thoughts of oh no… this is not going to go well moments. But… the way the author portrayed Clay’s journey, was simply heartbreakingly beautiful. He fought his awful demons with the help of his counselors, Aunt Ruby and of course Maggie- <b>“the one pure thing in his life.”</b><br><br>Healing did not happen overnight and nothing was a quick easy fix. Maggie and Clay started over in their relationship and even though I did not feel the excitement and intensity I did in the first book, I reflect now and think ‘wow… this is the way it should or would be- healing and recovery from crippling mental illness does not happen overnight and it never goes away. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401293i/778739.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Even though Clay and Maggie are fictional characters, I was full of pride over the maturity in which Clay handled his emotions and how he considered his health and well being over impulsive decisions.<br> He came to grips with his need for professional help and recognized that it would be something he had to deal with for a very long time.<br><br>The slow build to the end of the book was so worth it and even quite surprising. I did not predict the ending to play out the way it did and I have to say to Ms. Walters….lovely… <b>absolutely perfect!</b> <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/517106.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"The person who had always been my light in the shadows and who continued to love me even at my worst. Who reminded me that everyone deserved love, even me."</b>
</blockquote><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6351430346696015671" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_521376659" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/521376659" />
    <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty"><img alt="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481371426p2/13273769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/521376659?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty">Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer521376659" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2112671306116908076"><br/><b>"For those searching for the light…"<br/> "Never stop."<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795646._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>"Over six years ago I met a girl who saved me. I didn’t realize at the time, mostly because her attitude pissed me off, that she would become the most important thing in my life"<br/>"But then I got to know her and when I was drowning, she became my air. In the cold, she became my warmth.”<br/>"In the dark, she became my light,”"<br/></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795647.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Wow! God knows how long I've been waiting for this book! I was an absolute wreck after Find You In The Dark.<br/><br/><b>"The choices we make </b></span>
  <span id="freeText2112671306116908076" style="display:none"><br><b>"For those searching for the light…"<br> "Never stop."<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795646._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>"Over six years ago I met a girl who saved me. I didn’t realize at the time, mostly because her attitude pissed me off, that she would become the most important thing in my life"<br>"But then I got to know her and when I was drowning, she became my air. In the cold, she became my warmth.”<br>"In the dark, she became my light,”"<br></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795647.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wow! God knows how long I've been waiting for this book! I was an absolute wreck after Find You In The Dark.<br><br><b>"The choices we make in our life don't have to define us. It's what we learn from them that's important. You making the decisions that you did, while the fact that they were made in pain doesn't change, the outcomes are what you make of them"</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795648.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is such a special and beautifully written story! It picks up where the first book left off.<br>Clay now in a mental facility in Florida coping with his bipolar and personality disorder. He is so brave in his mental struggle... Every day is a fight, a fight sanity, to keep the pain away.. To fight the need not to cut. To easy the pain of loosing Maggie..<br><br><b>"I hated that my fucked up mind had taken something so wonderful and warped it into...well....something ugly."</b><br><br>Maggie is back home- 3 months later she is still trying to pick up the pieces after Clay left. After he broke her heart into a million pieces with the letter he sent telling her to move on with her life.<br>Sadness turned into anger is the only way Maggie is coping...<br><br>An unfortunate accident happens and Clay is forced to leave the Grayson Institute and go back 'home'<br><br>The problem is... Clay isn't strong enough for himself, let alone strong enough to be there for Ruby and his worst fear....to see Maggie again...<br><br><b>"The thing about the shadows is that they're not all darkness. You need to have light to have shadows. So just look for it,”"</b><br><br>The girl that will forever hold his heart, the girl he broke... Can he find his way back to her?<br><br><b>"I was an addict and Clay was my crack."</b><br><br>Offcourse Maggie and Clay cannot stay away from each other, like to magnets drawn to each other...<br><br><b>"There are times in our lives when you have to put aside what we think is best and go with what you feel is best.”<br>"I don’t want to wake up ten years from now regretting that I let this slip through my fingers. I don’t want to waste another moment without you in my life"</b><br><br>Maggie tells Clay exactly how she feels about him... Life is too short to waste these special feelings and moments...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795649.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"It’s because of everything we’ve been though that I can say it. I love you, Clayton Reed. God, I love you so damn much"<br><br>"I would never move on from Clay. My soul belonged with him, was so entangled in him that I was no longer a single being."</b><br><br>Love isn't the problem, it never was... Clay fights his inner demons. To change the Pattern...<br><br><b>"I think the person who said it’s better to have love and lost than to never have loved at all was full of shit."</b><br><br>Not to fall into the same things, this is a 2nd chance to do things right. Being without Maggie wasn't an option for Clay...<br><br><b><br>"You are everything good in my life. Even when I thought all I had was the darkness, you were there. And you gave me something to live for. I couldn’t let you go. No matter how hard I tried. I know now that’s because to lose you would be losing the very best part of myself.”</b><br><br><br>I am so incredibly proud of Clay! <br><br>He doesn't bottle up his emotions, he tells Maggie exactly what his feeling. They go to therapy together..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795650.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Its not the present that makes Clay crazy... Its the future<br><br>Faced with his demons again, he thinks his loosing Maggie to school and Ruby moving away... Clay is again that the same familiar cross road in his mind... To hurt himself or just DEAL with it..<br><br><b>"I’m not going anywhere. Because no one is abandoning you. People can move on and live their lives but that doesn’t mean you’re not a part of it anymore. I love you, Clay. Ruby loves you. Because you, Clay are worthy of that love. You deserve it. All of it."</b><br><br>I cannot commend A.Meredith Walters more! Fantastic writing in both Maggie and Clay's POVs! <br>We get to see the feelings from both sides. <br><br>Life isn't easy.. Love isn't always enough.. But Love conquers all.. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795651.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Looking down at Clay, his dark hair slicked back, his eyes radiating warmth and devotion, I knew that now, this love that had taken me to the highest heights and the lowest depths, that had terrified me and filled me with hope. This love between us was something I wanted to feel for the rest of my life."<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795652.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>"It’s a promise ring. A long time ago, they would be engraved with the words Pour route ma vie, de tout mon coeur, For my whole life, all of my love. I wanted to give you something that showed my complete and total devotion to you, to us."</b><br><br>So many emotions in this book! I loved loved every minute of it!!!<br><br>The ending was absolutely perfect!<br><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Again, Clay blew me away!!<br><br>Instead of pretending he was okay and everything was hunky dory, he knew what he had to do...<br>Instead of going on summer vacation with Maggie he made the decision to<br>Check himself back in at Grayson Institute for more treatment!He needed to do this for himself, to heal and to be the person he wanted to be for Maggie.<br>Clay asks Maggie to wait for him..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795653.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"I live and breathe for you. That I would lay down my life a million times over for you. And no matter what happens tomorrow, next week, next year, my heart will always be yours.”</b><br><br>Clay manned up! He took Charge Of His life! <br>I loved the fact that it wasn't a happy ending straight away! No ponies and rainbows!<br><br><b>"Life with Clayton Reed would never be sunshine and roses. It would be lots of shadows with intermittent light. And I was beginning to figure out ways to appreciate the light when I saw it. Because that darkness was still there. It most likely would always be there."</b><br><br>This was life and it was shitty and Clay dealt with it for Maggie and himself..<br><br>And it just gets better and better!!<br><br><b>"The Maggie and Clay story was far from over. And we would always be looking for the light…together"</b><br><br>The Epilogue!! Wow oh wow! <br>5years later Maggie and Clay are still together!!<br>Yay!!!!<br>This definitely was true love which WAS destined to be..<br><br><b>"Our road hasn’t been an easy one. But good things rarely are. You taught me that the person I am is worth loving, worth fighting for. You gave me strength when I had none. You held me up when I wanted to fall. And now, I want to give you everything. I want to give you the world. Because, Maggie, you’ve given me mine. And it’s you. It will always, forever, be you,”<br><br>"So together we walked into our future. One that we had mapped out. And that future was nothing but light"<br></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795654.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This heartbreaking, soul touching series Will stay with me for a long time.. And it's books like these that make us read &lt;3<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380750226ra/3119305.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/572876673" />
    <a title="Mo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11856352-mo"><img alt="Mo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371247812p2/11856352.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/572876673?book_show_action=true">Mar 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer572876673" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3491462428611019017">"Over six years ago, I met a girl who saved me .... I got to know her and when I was drowning, she became my air. In the cold, she became my warmth..... In the dark, she became my light."<br/><br/>Sigh. Well this was a rocky road to travel with the beautiful and troubled Clay and the fantastic Ms Maggie May. I will admit that I was disappointed with<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_' title='Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1359627731s/16081754.jpg' alt='Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> but really, really wanted to find out if Clay and Maggie got their pot of gold at the end of the rainbow. It was a tough road. You could feel the depths o</span>
  <span id="freeText3491462428611019017" style="display:none">"Over six years ago, I met a girl who saved me .... I got to know her and when I was drowning, she became my air. In the cold, she became my warmth..... In the dark, she became my light."<br><br>Sigh. Well this was a rocky road to travel with the beautiful and troubled Clay and the fantastic Ms Maggie May. I will admit that I was disappointed with<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_" title="Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1359627731s/16081754.jpg" alt="Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> but really, really wanted to find out if Clay and Maggie got their pot of gold at the end of the rainbow. It was a tough road. You could feel the depths of Clay's total mindset. Don't know anyone personally with bipolar, have read some books with characters that have it and have seen some TV shows where people are suffering from it. But Ms Walters seems to have done her research. His utter feeling of hopelessness came across totally. And the belief that Maggie had in him. Such a strong, strong girl. It was great. It was one of those books that leaves me with a headache, in a good way. Because I get so involved in the plot and characters I feel as if I am going through what they are going through. And on a final note, his f###ing parents, I mean seriously could people be more selfish. And Ruby, lovely Ruby - God only knows what he would have done without her. Off to find my next book now. Happy Easter Holidays to me and all of you.</span>

    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/480377102?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer480377102" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13958416362321579089"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401272i/778650._SX540_.jpg' width='300' height='275' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Light in the Shadows is a well done and completely believable conclusion to the book Find You in the Dark by A. Meredith Walters. It possessed pain, beauty, courage and light.<br/><br/>This book is written in alternating povs which gifted the reader the full scope of emotions both of our main characters felt from the first page. Their fears, anxiety, insecurities and most important a full look at what it’s like to struggle and live with mental illness. I related to Maggie, I to love someone who looks for</span>
  <span id="freeText13958416362321579089" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401272i/778650._SX540_.jpg" width="300" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Light in the Shadows is a well done and completely believable conclusion to the book Find You in the Dark by A. Meredith Walters. It possessed pain, beauty, courage and light.<br><br>This book is written in alternating povs which gifted the reader the full scope of emotions both of our main characters felt from the first page. Their fears, anxiety, insecurities and most important a full look at what it’s like to struggle and live with mental illness. I related to Maggie, I to love someone who looks for the light daily and I can honestly say that the author’s presentation of hospitalization, therapy and medication treatments are spot on.<br><br>This story is Clayton Reed’s road to the light. He is at Grayson Center and is enrolled in a 90 day program of medication, therapy and most important reframing. Clayton had let Maggie go at the end of Find You in the Dark and he struggles with what he did to their relationship as well as a gamut of emotions triggered by his illness. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I had turned on her. Turned on myself. And I had almost taken us both down in my delusions.”~ Clay</i>
</b><br><br>When tragedy strikes, Clayton finds himself back in Virginia. He sees how his actions affected Maggie and he tries desperately to become the man he always wanted to be while struggling to handle his illness. <br><br>I have read some reviews and I have to agree that Clay is wonderful but I loved Maggie just as much, her unwavering love is something to marvel at! <br><br>This story let a reader know that there are no quick fixes for mental illness, it is a daily struggle. The epilogue gave me the ending I had only dreamed for them in the first book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401272i/778651._SX540_.jpg" width="300" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13958416362321579089" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer591516882" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12526036131352999945"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 Beautiful STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383186741ra/6431941.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>"The thing about the shadows is that they're not all darkness. You need to have light to have shadows. Just look for it."<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br/>This story was heart achingly beautiful. So much has changed since the first book, and I am so happy to see the growth in both Maggie and Clay.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393448362i/8713888._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>After the way the first book ended--which in my opinion was for the best--I absolutely needed to know</span>
  <span id="freeText12526036131352999945" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 Beautiful STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383186741ra/6431941.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"The thing about the shadows is that they're not all darkness. You need to have light to have shadows. Just look for it."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>This story was heart achingly beautiful. So much has changed since the first book, and I am so happy to see the growth in both Maggie and Clay.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393448362i/8713888._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After the way the first book ended--which in my opinion was for the best--I absolutely needed to know <i>if</i> there would be a way for their relationship to work. Maggie is going through a "mourning" phase after Clay left. She doesn't know how Clay is doing at the facility, he has never tried to comunicate with her and she doesn't know how to communicate with him. She feels depressed, alone, and like her heart is completely shattered. Her friends Rachel and Daniel try to get her to move on and <i>live</i> her life. With time, she becomes stronger and more sure of herself. She still misses Clay and thinks she will always have a part of her that will love him always. But now she is taking the steps to move on.<br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“There is more beauty inside you than in anyone I have ever met. These pictures don’t lie. I won’t ever forget you. Or stop loving you. You can ask me to. You can tell me to move on. But I won’t. And I never will. Just don’t forget how beautiful we were. How beautiful we can still be.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>I understood where Maggie was coming from. I understood her sadness and anger. I felt for her because she knew absolutely nothing about Clay's well being. But I also very much wanted her to not continue to be consumed by him. I wanted her to find her independence and to learn how to make <i>herself</i> happy without needing Clay. I was happy that she had a support system in her friends and family. It was a slow progress but she did become more stronger. She was able to stand up for herself when she needed to.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You are everything good in my life. Even when I thought all I had was the darkness, you were there. And you gave ma something to live for. I couldn't let you go. No matter how hard I tried. I know now that's because to lose you would be losing the very best part of myself."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Clay is at a facility getting the help that he so desperately needed. He has made an amazing progress when compared to the guy he use to be. Each day is still a struggle for him. He still has bouts of depression, self-hatred, and the need to cut. But he has learned some coping methods to stay away from all that negativity. He is determined to become the man that Maggie deserves. He didn't fool himself into believing that he would be cured in three months. But he has gotten so much better.<br><br>I liked the way the author handled Clay's condition. The way Clay--even Maggie---grew, was really believable and really tough. It wasn't easy for them at all.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393447896i/8713791._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There was a tragedy that caused Clay and Maggie to reunite. I liked the way their relationship was rekindled and how they went slowly this time. They didn't go at it in a reckless hard and fast pace like in the last book. They thought long and hard before finally agreeing to try again. <br><br>I felt for Clay because the tragedy really affected him. But I liked that Clay really focused on his recovery, which is why he didn't want to burden Maggie by telling her how he was doing. Even when this tragedy struck, he still was able to call his doctor to chat about his feelings.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“My love for this beautifully broken, yet slowly healing boy, made me strong... I would never move on from Clay. My soul belonged with him, was so entangled in him that I was no longer a single being.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>I really appreciated Clay's POV--something we didn't have in the last book. I was able to understand him more. There were even a few glimpses of how he must have thought or felt in the first book that caused him to lose control. I liked how mature Maggie and Clay have become and seeing them learn how to handle their relationship. Since it was all so familiar to them, it was easy to fall back into their old ways that were destructive. They managed to stay strong, and I was so freaking happy about that.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393448465ra/8713932.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I love you, Maggie May Young. Always and forever.” And then my mouth touched hers and I felt my future begin.<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>They're journey to finding the light was a long one, and they still have a long way to go. I really enjoyed this second book more than the first. But the story as a whole was beautifully done. It was done in a realistic manner that caused me so much pain reading it. But it was all worth it in the end to see these two characters find happiness. It was an emotional ride, for sure. The only thing that still pisses me off is Clay's parents. I couldn't believe how they treated and continued to treat Clay. I am so happy Clay now has Maggie, Ruby, and his friends in his life. I was smiling so much with that ending. Especially the epilogue, I loved it! It was a great series. One you should give a try.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="12526036131352999945" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/573369152?book_show_action=true">Mar 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer573369152" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer350459357752554535">Brilliant! The only word for this book. 5++++++ stars. Awesome book happy dance going on here.....<br/><br/><b>"In the dark, she became my light."</b><br/><br/>This is a story of unconditional love, a story of trials in the face of mental illness, a story of healing and hope. Maggie and Clay have endured so much pain and turmoil in the face of his mental illness, it seems no relationship could survive it- at least not in any healthy way. <br/><br/>This book starts right up where the first book left off. Clay is living in an inpatie</span>
  <span id="freeText350459357752554535" style="display:none">Brilliant! The only word for this book. 5++++++ stars. Awesome book happy dance going on here.....<br /><br /><b>"In the dark, she became my light."</b><br /><br />This is a story of unconditional love, a story of trials in the face of mental illness, a story of healing and hope. Maggie and Clay have endured so much pain and turmoil in the face of his mental illness, it seems no relationship could survive it- at least not in any healthy way. <br /><br />This book starts right up where the first book left off. Clay is living in an inpatient mental hospital trying to cope with his Bipolar and Personality Disorder. Maggie is back in Virginia trying to put the pieces of her life back together sans Clay. He's essentially cut off all contact with her other than the Dear John letter he sent her. Maggie still loves him but is angry he took the easy way out by cutting her off completely. Ten weeks and no contact. Ten weeks of looks from everyone at school, the girl who's boyfriend tried to off himself. She's gotta pull it together. <br /><br />When an unfortunate family emergency forces Clay to leave Grayson Institute and return to VA, Maggie has to face seeing Clay again. Her feelings are mixed. She misses him, loves him, but is angry with him. Clay knows he's no good for Maggie but he's a selfish guy and cannot resist talking to her. The chemistry between them is like it has always been....palpable. <br /><br />Can these two get past all the hurt they've caused each other, their families, their friends? Can Clay make it on the outside or should he return to Grayson where he truly needs to be? He's torn between family responsibilities and self healing. <br /><br />I cannot commend the author enough for this book. She brought to light the trials of mental illness, not sugar coating or dramatizing it, just giving us the reality of what living with and loving a person with mental illness is like. I had no idea. I felt so much empathy for both of them. Maggie, for being a young 17 years old was so mature and supportive of all things Clay. She was his reason for everything. I don't think he would've made it without her love and support. Clay, I loved his commitment to his Aunt Ruby and Maggie, putting his own needs on hold to help them when they needed it. But also for realizing he needed to take care of his own demons if he's going to be able have a healthy relationship with Maggie. He saw his limitations and he did something about it. Even if it wasn't the easy way out. <br /><br />Such a great conclusion to an extremely angsty book full of emotions and mental strife. This will be a book I carry with me for a long time to come.....<br /><br /><br /></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_486958282" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/486958282" />
    <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578074503p2/8524618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/486958282?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads">Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer486958282" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11499335583588542958"><a href='http://www.angiesdreamyreads.com/2013/04/blog-tour-light-in-shadows-by-ameredith.html?spref=fb' rel='nofollow noopener'>This review was posted at Angie's Dreamy Reads!!</a><br/><br/><i>Win an eBook copy of this book by clicking on the link above</i><br/><br/><b>4.5 INCREDIBLE STARS</b><br/><br/>After reading the first book in this series Find You in The Dark I was completely in love with A. Meredith Walters writing and characters. The first book left me in complete agony wanting to know how Maggie and Clay were going to heal from what they had just experienced with each other, and how Clay was going to be able to put his life back together and overcome all of </span>
  <span id="freeText11499335583588542958" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.angiesdreamyreads.com/2013/04/blog-tour-light-in-shadows-by-ameredith.html?spref=fb" rel="nofollow noopener">This review was posted at Angie's Dreamy Reads!!</a><br /><br /><i>Win an eBook copy of this book by clicking on the link above</i><br /><br /><b>4.5 INCREDIBLE STARS</b><br /><br />After reading the first book in this series Find You in The Dark I was completely in love with A. Meredith Walters writing and characters. The first book left me in complete agony wanting to know how Maggie and Clay were going to heal from what they had just experienced with each other, and how Clay was going to be able to put his life back together and overcome all of the SERIOUS issues that plagued him. If you haven’t read the first book in the series I would ABSOLUTELY recommend you do so. It’s a story of a boy who is suffering with Bipolar and several other issues that stem from that. Maggie is someone that he has an uncanny connection to. Their relationship is extremely toxic and harmful to both of them. It’s hard to read as its extremely angsty and heartbreaking. These two have a love for each other that’s very deep. When it comes to Clay, Maggie is a nurturer. All she wants to do is be the source of healing for this boy that she has fallen so madly and deeply in love with. The problem is that Clay doesn’t have a handle on his issues and they go beyond his control, setting up a disaster waiting to happen.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"The choices we make in our lives don’t define us. It’s what we learn from them that’s important.” </b>
</i> <br /><br />When we left Clay and Maggie last they were both separated from each other. Clay is now in a 90 day treatment facility that is helping him find ways to cope with life and his disorders as well as helping him get his meds under control. He’s had no contact with Maggie and has sent her a letter telling her to move on. Clay has learned in therapy that Maggie is a trigger for him that could send him spiraling in the wrong direction leading him into the same toxic lifestyle that he wants so desperately to get away from. Knowing that is hard for Clay to accept but he WANTS more than anything to be whole and not known as the crazy kid that could lose his shit at any moment.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"My feelings about Maggie May Young were too intense, too consuming and they always threatened to swallow me whole.” -Clay </b>
</i><br /><br />Maggie (sweet, sweet Mags....I really do love her) is STRUGGLING to move past Clay. The thought of her life without him is unbearable at times but she knows she needs to pick herself up and move on. The problem between knowing you need to do something and actually doing it is the thing that she’s stuck on. She’s angry at Clay for abandoning her and just giving up on their relationship but at the same time understands that he needs to “fix himself”.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"Seeing him again had only confirmed what my subconscious already knew. I would never move on from Clay. My soul belonged with him, was so entangled in him that I was no longer a single being.” - Maggie </b>
</i><br /><br />An unexpected event happens that leads Clayton out of rehab and back to town. When Maggie and Clay come face to face their lives are inexplicably changed again. Even though things have changed between them while they were separated, a lot stayed the same. The pull they have to each other is still strong and unwavering and the need for each other and love they have still burns bright. There is SO much baggage and trouble that they have to face and learn to deal with. So many issues that Clay has yet to work through and fix. It’s a bumpy ride but so good and so worth every moment of pain and sadness.<br /> <br /><i>
  <b>"You are everything good in my life. Even when I thought all I had was the darkness, you were there. And you gave me something to live for. I couldn’t let you go. No matter how hard I tried. I know now that’s because to lose you would be like losing the very best part of myself.” - Clay </b>
</i><br /><br />These two characters are very dear to my heart. Clay and Maggie are both a joy to read about. I love them so much. I understood so much of what they were going through and what they desperately needed from each other. It’s amazing that when you love someone a monumental shift takes place in your life. There's no denying true love whether is be selfish or not and for Maggie and Clay when they fell in love there was a HUGE change in how they lived their lives and how it affected their day to day. The dynamic between the two of them is intense and deep. It’s all consuming and unhealthy at times but nonetheless there and ever present. I LOVE them. I just really do. <br /><br /><br />Out of all the characters I’ve ever read about I think Clay might be the most inspirational. This boy has a WALK IN sized closet worth of issues. In life Clay has gotten the short end of the stick, between his mental health, parents and the hand he’s dealt as far as tragedy goes, he’s has it rough!!! BUT his determination to change his life, do the WORK and LISTEN to his therapist has him making HUGE strides. Eventually after lots of work he learns to manage and control his condition and that really shows how exceptional of a person he is. You can do ANYTHING that you put your mind to. Life is work but no matter what the choice is YOURS!!! You either let it beat you or you beat it and Clay....He works HARD to beat it and get it under control. Is he perfect NO but he gets back up and tries again and that makes me love him even more. <br /><br />Overall I thought this was a FANTASTIC continuation of the series. It was heartwarming and inspirational. This is one of my most favorite series because it’s not fluffy and wrapped in a bow!! It’s real and the characters have REAL issues that I thought the author worked through brilliantly. I would HIGHLY recommend this book and the first. It’s a gripping tale of how severe mental issues can be but also offers a HOPE that there is light in those dark shadows and you CAN pick yourself up no matter the situation. I LOVED it. Maggie and Clayton are absolutely AMAZING. <br /><br /><i>I was provided and ARC of this book for an honest review </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="11499335583588542958" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_480500565" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/480500565" />
    <a title="Kirsty" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10389044-kirsty"><img alt="Kirsty" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1409522343p2/10389044.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/480500565?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kirsty" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kirsty" href="/user/show/10389044-kirsty">Kirsty</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10389044-kirsty?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer480500565" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2495181787472136805"><b>*3.5 stars*</b><br/><br/>I really, really hate it when I don't like a book half as much as all my bookie friends did, but that's what happened here with LITS. I can't put my finger on what it is I don't like about this series but I felt the same with FYITD too. Maybe it's Maggie, or the fact it seems way too long with too much inner dialogue. I don't know. It just doesn't work for me. <br/><br/>Anyway.. I love Clay ALOT. One of the only reasons I continued with this series is because I wanted Clay to find his HAE. I do</span>
  <span id="freeText2495181787472136805" style="display:none"><b>*3.5 stars*</b><br /><br />I really, really hate it when I don't like a book half as much as all my bookie friends did, but that's what happened here with LITS. I can't put my finger on what it is I don't like about this series but I felt the same with FYITD too. Maybe it's Maggie, or the fact it seems way too long with too much inner dialogue. I don't know. It just doesn't work for me. <br /><br />Anyway.. I love Clay ALOT. One of the only reasons I continued with this series is because I wanted Clay to find his HAE. I don't think there's ever been a character deserve it more than him. I love how in this book he is finally taking care of himself and really is interested in keeping himself healthy. I hated seeing him go through so many breakdowns in FYITD so this was such a good change. <br /><br />As for Maggie.. I just don't like her. I'm not sure if its her age that bothers me but she just seems to immature. Granted she had grown up a ton in this book so it was really good to see that but there's still something about her that bugs the hell out of me. I have to give her credit for never wavering in her love for Clay though.. and this time around she didn't compromise his health once. <br /><br />All in all I think if you enjoyed FYITD then you will LOVE this series but as I've said it just really wasn't for me. I'd even go as far to say that I'm glad it's over now, but maybe that's just me..<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"When I was drowning, she became my air. In the cold, she became my warmth. In the dark, she became my light."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17494287428613625581"><b>♥ 5- WONDERFUL, MESMERIZING, AMAZINGLY BEAUTIFUL, EARTH-SHATTERING STARS. ♥</b><br/><br/><br/>After reading the first book in this series Find You in The Dark I was completely in love with A. Meredith Walters writing and characters. The first book left me in complete agony wanting to know how Maggie and Clay were going to heal from what they had just experienced with each other, and how Clay was going to be able to put his life back together and overcome all of the SERIOUS issues that plagued him.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402335i/781924.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/> <b>"My feelings abo</b></span>
  <span id="freeText17494287428613625581" style="display:none"><b>♥ 5- WONDERFUL, MESMERIZING, AMAZINGLY BEAUTIFUL, EARTH-SHATTERING STARS. ♥</b><br><br><br>After reading the first book in this series Find You in The Dark I was completely in love with A. Meredith Walters writing and characters. The first book left me in complete agony wanting to know how Maggie and Clay were going to heal from what they had just experienced with each other, and how Clay was going to be able to put his life back together and overcome all of the SERIOUS issues that plagued him.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402335i/781924.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br> <b>"My feelings about Maggie May Young were too intense, too consuming and they always threatened to swallow me whole.”</b> -Clay <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402335i/781925._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While Clay is recovering at a mental institution, and finally receiving proper guidance for his illness, Maggie tries to put back together the broken pieces of her life. Every day Clay misses Maggie. She was the one who fueled his jealousy and rage, but she is also the one who was and always will be his light in the dark.<br><br><br>I cried my way through the epilogue and when I finished the book, I literally just sat there with tears pouring down my face for several minutes... just over flowing with emotions ??<br><br><br>And at the end as Clay believed Maggie's love did saved him.<br><br><b>“My love for this beautifully broken, yet slowly healing boy, made me strong…. My soul belonged with him, was so entangled in him that I was no longer a single being.”</b><br><br><b>“It was just two people who loved each other, trying to make some sense in a world where there was none.”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402335i/781926.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Clay and Maggie's story will remain in my heart forever ?<br><br><b>"You are everything good in my life. Even when I had thought all I had was the darkness... you gave me something to live for."</b><br><br><br>Such a great conclusion to an extremely angsty book full of emotions and mental strife. This will be a book I carry with me for a long time <br>to come.....<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402335i/781927.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_630990728" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/630990728" />
    <a title="Shell The Belle " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15880350-shell-the-belle"><img alt="Shell The Belle " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1399759491p2/15880350.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/630990728?book_show_action=true">Jun 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shell The Belle " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shell The Belle " href="/user/show/15880350-shell-the-belle">Shell The Belle </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15880350-shell-the-belle?shelf=book-lovers-i-love-to-love">book-lovers-i-love-to-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15880350-shell-the-belle?shelf=book-boys-i-love-so-much">book-boys-i-love-so-much</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15880350-shell-the-belle?shelf=favourite-books-of-all-time">favourite-books-of-all-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15880350-shell-the-belle?shelf=deserves-all-the-hype">deserves-all-the-hype</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer630990728" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3064884821026504785"><b>FOUR HEART-WRENCHING STARS</b><br/><br/><br/>Firstly, what a FANTASTIC book cover!! This is exactly how I picture Clayton Reed!<br/><br/>Well, I have to admit, i really loved this book. In a way, I didn't want it to end. I found that I liked it a lot more than <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_' title='Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters' rel='nofollow noopener'>Find You in the Dark</a>. I don't usually like stories with a strong illness storyline, and in this case it is mental illness. Clay self harms, and at times it has been near fatal. But this story, this story just had me hooked from book one, and this second is better stil</span>
  <span id="freeText3064884821026504785" style="display:none"><b>FOUR HEART-WRENCHING STARS</b><br><br><br>Firstly, what a FANTASTIC book cover!! This is exactly how I picture Clayton Reed!<br><br>Well, I have to admit, i really loved this book. In a way, I didn't want it to end. I found that I liked it a lot more than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_" title="Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">Find You in the Dark</a>. I don't usually like stories with a strong illness storyline, and in this case it is mental illness. Clay self harms, and at times it has been near fatal. But this story, this story just had me hooked from book one, and this second is better still. <br><br>I wont go into too much detail of the story, the blurb and other reviews do that nicely. But this is what I thought.<br><br>The message in this book is a strong and realistic one;<br><br><b>LOVE IS <u>NOT</u> ALWAYS ENOUGH.</b><br><br>This was apparent at the end of the first book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_" title="Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">Find You in the Dark</a> and is re-iterated in this one. So many YA/NA books make out that if you love someone enough everything will be okay. Love is seen as a cure for so many things: <br><br><b>It's not. It almost never is. Love isn't a miracle cure, It cant solve all of life's problems, and it wont cure illness - mental or otherwise.</b> It can help a person or persons be stronger, to deal with adversity, or give someone a different, better perspective on things/life. Some would say it gives life meaning, and I would agree with that. What it <b>wont do</b> is change an abusive partner/relationship, (not that this story is about an abusive relationship, btw) or pay the bills, or cure all life's illnesses/woes, etc etc. And that is the message this book gives. <br><br>Clay and Maggie love each other but that love alone will never be enough to stop Clay self destructing. Mental illness, particularly amongst the young, is still pretty much unknown territory, but A. Meredith Walters dealt with it brilliantly in this heartbreaking story. <br><br>I really did like the duel perspective this time, too. It was fascinating getting into Clay's head. I really, really felt for his character and by 20% in I <b>
  <i>loved</i>
</b> him (not in the book boyfriend way but just as a character!) It is so sad that there are kids going through this kind of thing and at times this book really makes your heart ACHE!! <br><br><a href="http://s1086.photobucket.com/user/64_bit/media/tumblr_lktblkcz581qc0shi.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/236719.gif" alt="crying .gif photo tumblr_lktblkcz581qc0shi.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It was all very believable. The knowledge and research of the subject matter was second to none. I was able to identify with both characters, although I liked Clay's character more than I did Maggie. I think I just found Maggie too out of touch with his condition and what state of mind he had been in when he sent her "the letter" at the beginning and she made too much of it, given what he had just been through. <br><a href="http://www.threadbombing.com/details.php?image_id=3600" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/234001.gif" alt="Cry" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br>And throughout the second half of the book she was planning on doing stuff that as a reader I just knew would be sending Clay back to the edge. I kept on thinking, knowing your partners state of mind, and what he has been through, is this the wisest thing to expect? I think though that simply showed Maggie's immaturity, she was only eighteen, after all.<br><br>I must admit If I was Maggie's parents, I wouldn't want her to have anything to do with a character like Clay, because I would justifiably fear for her future with someone like that. <br><br>I was 88% done with the book and I still didn't know how it was going to all work out! Clay's character IS exhausting, and I don't think, in reality, anyone could stand the pace and stay the course in a relationship with someone like him. Maggie is young, its all so easy to make lifelong decisions when you are so young and not realise that they are simply too hard or not achievable. But anything can happen I guess. The book keeps you guessing to the very end, and I <b>LOVED</b> that about it. <br><br><br>Not sure about the very last chapter - I am not going to give anything away because if you haven't read these two books I thoroughly recommend them - but lets just say it is what I would hope for but even then, would it be a practical reality for Maggie?? I am not so sure. Like I said, she is young.<br><br><b>All in all I really enjoyed reading this, but would recommend with caution as there are disturbing elements to the story.<br><br>But most definitely a <u>SHELL YES!</u> from me.</b> <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=350jx9k" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423856ra/844694.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="3064884821026504785" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2545624925" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2545624925" />
    <a title="Lo Bookfrantic" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14746493-lo-bookfrantic"><img alt="Lo Bookfrantic" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1450644315p2/14746493.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

<div id="review_599094125" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/599094125" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/599094125?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=oh-the-angst">oh-the-angst</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer599094125" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer468905634064274829"> <i> <b> “For my whole life, all of my love.”</b></i><br/><br/>This story picks up a few months after Clay sent Maggie the letter telling her to be free and move on and after he has been admitted in Greystone for treatment. <br/>He is miserable but still thinks that he made the best option letting her free and that she’s way better off without him and his problems. The thing is… Maggie didn’t move on. She’s in a bad place without him and doesn’t know or want to move on from Clay. <br/>Until the day that an unfortunate event make</span>
  <span id="freeText468905634064274829" style="display:none"> <i> <b> “For my whole life, all of my love.”</b></i><br><br>This story picks up a few months after Clay sent Maggie the letter telling her to be free and move on and after he has been admitted in Greystone for treatment. <br>He is miserable but still thinks that he made the best option letting her free and that she’s way better off without him and his problems. The thing is… Maggie didn’t move on. She’s in a bad place without him and doesn’t know or want to move on from Clay. <br>Until the day that an unfortunate event make Clay take the decision to come home again and they find each other one more time. The feelings that never left are stronger than ever and Clay knows that he already made too many mistakes to try to ask for Maggie’s forgiveness. And Maggie is scared that all the things that happened before will come back because she knows she can’t go through all that again.<br>But Clay is better, on new meds and things seem slightly better than before, and since they apparently can’t stay away from each other… they try again. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418929i/829942._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their story isn’t simpler in this book… is just less angsty because they already know what to expect from Clay and they aren’t hiding his problems anymore. I really loved to see how Maggie’s friends and parents, even with all reservations, accepted Clay back in their life’s and supported Maggie in every way possible. <br>Their love is once more beautiful to see and is impossible not to fall in love with the two of them together. And they try really hard to be happy but dark clouds are still in the sky and things can go wrong at any time. So they just try to enjoy what they have together while Clay’s find a way to be possible to have a future with Maggie. <br><br><i> <b>“I wish I could say that one day things might be simpler. But the truth is I can’t say that. I wish I could. I can only say, with one hundred percent certainty that I love you. That I live and breathe for you. That I would lay down my life a million times over for you. And no matter what happens tomorrow, next week, next year, my heart will always be yours”<br></b></i><br><br> This second book is simply amazing. I loved to see an ending to their sad story and find a way to end up together. I especially love how their love never died even with all the obstacles and problems they had to go through. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418929ra/829943.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One of those books that will stay with me for a long time.<br>Go read it now, people! :)<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="468905634064274829" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5606933-that-s-all-ash?shelf=omg">omg</a>
          </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16143475964954082429"><b>
  <i> …’Cause I am hanging<br/>On every word you say<br/>And even if you don’t want to speak tonight<br/>That’s alright… alright with me.<br/><br/>‘Cause I want nothing more<br/>Than to <br/>Sit outside Heaven’s door<br/>And listen to your breathing…</i>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_m1k70pE9rz1qk9wb4o1_500.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText16143475964954082429" style="display:none"><b>
  <i> …’Cause I am hanging<br>On every word you say<br>And even if you don’t want to speak tonight<br>That’s alright… alright with me.<br><br>‘Cause I want nothing more<br>Than to <br>Sit outside Heaven’s door<br>And listen to your breathing…</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_m1k70pE9rz1qk9wb4o1_500.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>-:- FOUR ASTRONOMICAL STARS! -:-<br><br>When we last left Clay and Maggie… all Maggie was left of the scarred boy was the memory of him with thick bandages on his wrists, laying in a hospital bed; and a good-bye letter fluttering in her hand.<br><br>And then<i>Light in the Shadows</i> begins.<br><br>Clay is now in a treatment facility, trying to gain higher ground over his inner demons. And he’s finally succeeding with his new medication; new friends; and therapists. It’s a 90 day program, and he’s made it and is even contemplating staying longer to further his efforts.<br><br>But he still can’t forget about her.<br><br>Maggie.<br><br>The girl whose world he completely annihilated along with his own as she tried to save him. The girl with the gorgeous brown eyes and the soul of a titanium butterfly. The girl who sends him an emotional heart-searing gift on his birthday despite his good-bye letter.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_lwosv58B7f1qlccb8o1_1280.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>And only when Clayton Reed finally begins to understand that the only way he could be with the girl who is impossible to forget does he begin to truly begin to understand how crucial his recovery is.<br><br>Until something happens that sends all that understanding careening into the wind.<br><br>And that <i>something</i> brings the war-like Clayton Reed face to face with the casualty-like Maggie Young once again.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/6754899541_c9f65e8ce9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>Clay’s back in town. Just when Maggie has dusted herself off from the hell of a fall three months ago. She followed a beautiful boy into the shadows, and came back a little bit stronger and little more damaged.<br><br>She still loves him and craves him and wants him.<br><br><b>
  <i> “There is more beauty inside you than in anyone I have ever met. These pictures don’t lie. I won’t ever forget you. Or stop loving you. You can ask me to. You can tell me to move on. But I won’t. And I never will. Just don’t forget how beautiful we were. How beautiful we can still be.” -- Maggie </i>
</b><br><br>And so they give it another go. But this time, it’s different. Because Clay is half-way recovered and doesn’t want it to be about him anymore. He wants it to be about Maggie. About deserving her. <br><br>But the thing about recovery is… is that when you’re half-way to recovery, you’re half-way to a relapse.<br><br>So will she love him to restoration?<br>Or will he love her to ruins?<br><br>Grab some alcohol and your favorite security blanket… because there’s only one way to find out. ;) <br><br><b>
  <i>As much as I missed her and dreamed of this moment, I was scared of it. Too much had changed. Yet seeing her, my heart and body reacted the same as it always had. She had been my crutch and now she was something else entirely, a painful reminder of all the ways I screwed up. But watching my gorgeous girl move through the crowd of people, I only saw the person I had pinned my future on. And that was both exhilarating and terrifying.</i>
</b><br></span>
