<div id="review_480496565" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/480496565" />
    <a title="Kim Person" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7590856-kim-person"><img alt="Kim Person" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1434694589p2/7590856.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/480496565?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kim Person" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kim Person" href="/user/show/7590856-kim-person">Kim Person</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7590856-kim-person?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7590856-kim-person?shelf=beta">beta</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer480496565" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7070940312274683059">I DISTINCTLY remember the day I got the ARC for Light In the Shadows! I was a HUGE fan of Maggie & Clay's from Find You in the Dark and to receive an ARC for this one left me well.............................<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401291ra/778730.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>and when I was able to recover from my little episode I was..........<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401291ra/778731.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>obviously I was BEYOND excited to see what would happen with Maggie & Clay especially after the end of Find You in the Dark! The book opens with Clay's POV and we see that he is in an in-resident treatment center trying to </span>
  <span id="freeText7070940312274683059" style="display:none">I DISTINCTLY remember the day I got the ARC for Light In the Shadows! I was a HUGE fan of Maggie &amp; Clay's from Find You in the Dark and to receive an ARC for this one left me well.............................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401291ra/778730.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and when I was able to recover from my little episode I was..........<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401291ra/778731.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>obviously I was BEYOND excited to see what would happen with Maggie &amp; Clay especially after the end of Find You in the Dark! The book opens with Clay's POV and we see that he is in an in-resident treatment center trying to learn to "live" with his mental illness. He seemed to be doing pretty darn good when it started but I was also very.........<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/515302.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>see Clay convinced himself he wasn't "good enough" for Maggie and he needed to stay away from her. He hadn't called her, wrote to her heck she had NO idea where he was! We get to re-live what this has been like for Maggie who basically felt like this once Clay was removed from her life..................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401291ra/778732.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>but will Maggie be able to move forward with her life? Can she enjoy things she once did before without Clay? Without the one boy she is convinced she will always love and there would never be another? Well, my friends you have to read that to find out but don't under estimate the POWER of this story. Don't for one second think this is going to be a ride that's all sweet and fluffy! It can't be that way to be true to form and to "experience" the book! What ultimately brings Clay back town had me..........................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/252540.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh yes!! I was a sobbing mess ~ I swear my heart literally hurt! Well I finally had Maggie &amp; Clay in the same generally vincinity now it was time for me to cross my fingers and PRAY that something would happen, well something good that is ~ Now I honestly can say that for most of the book I was alternating between..................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/587868.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and of course this.................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401291ra/778733.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Of course there were times where I ..................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401291ra/778734.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and when a "friend" of Clay's from rehab comes to visited I did....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380350752ra/704494.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Watching Maggie &amp; Clay slowly dance around one another and then thinking all would be made me feel like I was in a jumpy house ~ up one minute and down the next! The decision Clay makes, which I have to give him huge KUDOS for, had me.....................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397950ra/768516.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and then boy oh boy I was right back to..............................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401291ra/778735.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't think the book would've worked for me if this didn't happen. I loved the decision he made even if Maggie didn't but I also loved that this gave Clay what he really needed actually had to have to learn to really live with his disease because without it I don't think I would've got and ending that had me...................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/416073.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Light In the Shadows was Beyond Amazing!!!!!!! Clay &amp; Maggie's story will grip you HARD!!! I'm still living this one and I finished the book quite awhile ago. There is NO way you could limit this to only 5 stars ~ LITS is far beyond a 5 star read!!! <br><br>It's BRILLIANT AMAZING GUT-WRENCHING ~ I was 100% emotionally invested in this book! I experienced each and every one of the emotions displayed in the book. I forgot it was a story I really did I felt that I was a "part" of Maggie &amp; Clay's lives and that everything that had transpired I had lived with them. I had moments of very deep despair for what Clay had been through and continued to live through. I felt for Maggie but admired her "strength" and "courage" to ultimately fight for what she wanted and knew she could have with Clay. I'm absolutely THRILLED with the way the book ended and there's not a darn thing I would change about this one! I'm also very sad that it appears Maggie &amp; Clay's journey is over ~ I felt like I just said goodbye to some very good friends.<br><br>If you haven't read Find You in the Dark I encourage you to move this up your TBR, buy it and begin this FANTASTIC series! Get to know not only Maggie &amp; Clay but the other wonderful supporting characters in the book. You will adore Daniel and Rachel and many more. Now if you've read Find You in the Dark then I just have to say YOU NEED TO READ LIGHT IN THE SHADOWS NOW.......... NO putting this one off anymore ~ grab it and read it Right.Freaking.Now! You will not be sorry! This is one of my ALL time favorite reads that I can guarantee I will be re-visiting time and time again!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7070940312274683059" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_514404647" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/514404647" />
    <a title="Chris- Bookaddict" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4949749-chris--bookaddict"><img alt="Chris- Bookaddict" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451243308p2/4949749.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/514404647?book_show_action=true">Jan 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chris- Bookaddict" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chris- Bookaddict" href="/user/show/4949749-chris--bookaddict">Chris- Bookaddict</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer514404647" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10055368400479357199"><a href='http://imgur.com/Kd2toUI' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406360i/792687._SX540_.jpg' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I fell in love with Maggie and Clay in Finding You in the Dark. As dysfunctional as I thought they were, I knew they would over come their shadows and there would be a light at the end of their tunnel . <br/><br/>This Book Was Incredible , It gave Maggie and Clay their light at the end of the tunnel and I enjoyed the journey to that light with them both. <br/><br/>This was one hell of a bumpy road , but it was also the most amazing journey I had ever been on with a book series . The healing, the trying to cope </span>
  <span id="freeText10055368400479357199" style="display:none"><a href="http://imgur.com/Kd2toUI" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406360i/792687._SX540_.jpg" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I fell in love with Maggie and Clay in Finding You in the Dark. As dysfunctional as I thought they were, I knew they would over come their shadows and there would be a light at the end of their tunnel . <br><br>This Book Was Incredible , It gave Maggie and Clay their light at the end of the tunnel and I enjoyed the journey to that light with them both. <br><br>This was one hell of a bumpy road , but it was also the most amazing journey I had ever been on with a book series . The healing, the trying to cope in the outside world, the recovery. It was amazing. <br><br>Clay , he was amazing, He loved Maggie with his whole heart, and he fought for that love by working to fix "himself" . As much as he felt like giving in so many times , he knew that he wanted that Happiness at the end of the tunnel with Maggie and by jesus he fought for it all the way to the end . <br><br>Maggie , I loved her I truly did , a couple times I will admit she did tick me off , with the whole (are you taking your meds) every time Clay had a moment, But as I read more of the story I understood where she was coming from and I understood that she had to re-build that trust that she had in Clay . The fact that she stood by him through it all Just swooned my heart for both of them completely. I loved watching them both work through things "together" , that in itself was amazing and showed truly how much she loved Clay with all her heart, and just how much Clay truly loved her. <br><br><br>"For a guy who struggled with finding his place in the world, standing next to Maggie, I understood one thing on a very fundamental level. Wherever she went, whatever she did, that is where I belonged." <br> <br><br>Book Blurb:<br><br>How do you keep going when you feel like your life is over?<br><br>Maggie never thought she’d see Clay again. So, she attempts to put her life back together after her heart has been shattered to pieces. Moving on and moving forward, just as Clay wanted her to.<br><br>Clay never stopped thinking of Maggie. Even after ripping their lives apart and leaving her behind to get the help he so desperately needed. He is healing...slowly. But his heart still belongs to the girl who tried to save him.<br><br>When a sudden tragedy brings Maggie and Clay face to face again, nothing is the same. Yet some things never change. Can the darkness that threatened to consume them be transformed into something else and finally give them what they always wanted? And can two people who fought so hard to be together, finally find their happiness? Or will their demons and fear drive them apart for good?<br><br>The thing about love, is even when it destroys you, it has a way of mending what is broken. And in the shadows, you can still see the light<br><br><br>There is an Epilogue I cried my way through it, I was hanging onto every last word and I wanted more of Clay and Maggie, they do get their happy ending and it is the most amazing one . I loved every word of it all the way to the end. <br><br>"God I loved her... She was everything I wanted in my life but was still unsure I deserved... I wanted this. And I wanted to run from it. I wanted to pull her in and never let go. I wanted to push her away... I wanted to taste her skin and feel her heart beat beneath my lips." <br><br><br>This was the most amazing journey I have ever been on in a book series, The author did an upstanding job of bringing these two characters to life in this series. You literally feel every emotion with them through the whole ride. <br><br>If you have not read this series yet , you don't know what you are missing . Hands down one of the best series ever . <br><br><br><br>"You are everything good in my life. Even when I had thought all I had was the darkness... you gave me something to live for." </span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8707782-aimen?shelf=read-over-and-over">read-over-and-over</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8707782-aimen?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8707782-aimen?shelf=swoon-worthy-guys">swoon-worthy-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8707782-aimen?shelf=cover-lust">cover-lust</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8707782-aimen?shelf=good-girl-bad-boy">good-girl-bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8707782-aimen?shelf=alternate-povs">alternate-povs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8707782-aimen?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8707782-aimen?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8707782-aimen?shelf=deserves-six-stars">deserves-six-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8707782-aimen?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer587222594" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1088632332630793096"><b>*5 LIGHT AND DARK STARS*</b><br/><br/>So...wow. This book definitely got to me in all the right places. I mean I'm still struck by that super-duper-epicly-fantastical HEA so I will try to write a good review. My thoughts are all over the place but here goes.<br/><br/><b>"In the dark, she became my light.” </b><br/><br/>This is the second book to the series Find you in the Dark. The first book I could only give 4 stars because of some pretty big issues. For one thing, Clay had some really annoying anger issues. Like one minute he was al</span>
  <span id="freeText1088632332630793096" style="display:none"><b>*5 LIGHT AND DARK STARS*</b><br><br>So...wow. This book definitely got to me in all the right places. I mean I'm still struck by that super-duper-epicly-fantastical HEA so I will try to write a good review. My thoughts are all over the place but here goes.<br><br><b>"In the dark, she became my light.” </b><br><br>This is the second book to the series Find you in the Dark. The first book I could only give 4 stars because of some pretty big issues. For one thing, Clay had some really annoying anger issues. Like one minute he was all "God Maggie, mind you're own business! I know you're trying to help but blah blah blah blah blah!" Yeah, okay. And then the next he was all "I'm so sorry baby. I have anger issues. <s>Clearly.</s> Please forgive me!" And then Maggie's all "I looked into his eyes and just...<i>melted</i>" Ohmagod, that word! MELTED. It was everywhere. Basically, both of their emotions were all over the place. It was hard to keep up and quite frankly, gave me a headache.<br><br>This book, however, improved <i>drastically!</i> Like you-deserve-six-stars drastically. For one thing, I think adding Clay's POV really helped us understand why he had such mind-racking mood swings. We got an inside look into this yummy boy's head! Though the emotions were still all over the place, I guess you could say this book was more understandable. Like I know Clay and Maggie were in the dark but all their bickering put ME in the dark as well. Just saying. This time, Clay really shone through! He was trying above and beyond for Maggie and well, no one could resist that. If you're a woman then you <i>will</i> fall for Clay and his dark, mysterious, and luring side. If not then there is something incredibly wrong with you. He was so sweet and good to Maggie in this one. He stayed on his meds, went to therapy and did anything if it meant making the two of them work.<br><br><b>“For a guy who struggled with finding his place in the world, standing next to Maggie, I understood one thing on a very fundamental level. Wherever she went, whatever she did, that is where I belonged.”</b><br><br>Maggie also really developed as a character in this book. She went from whiny, bratty, defensive, you-don't-know-the-love-i-share-with-clay-girl to the WOMAN who became stronger and took in everything with her head held high. Sure she still loved Clay after all that (who wouldn't?) but she spoke her mind and actually called him out when he treated her like total BS. And Clay understood, did his best to right his wrongs. Their relationship was full of understanding and support and <b>light</b> whereas in the previous one it was too <b>dark.</b><br><br>All in all, I really enjoyed this one! Definitely goes in my deserves-six-stars shelf! Their HEA was the sweetest one I've read about so far. It was perfect and completely satisfying for all you fans out there. I think Walters really shone in writing this heart-wrenching, gut-twisting, tear-jerking story. I'm so pleased with how this ended! (It is the last one right?) I couldn't have asked for a more perfect conclusion to this series.<br><br><b>“I love you, Maggie May Young. Always and forever.” And then my mouth touched hers and I felt my future begin.” </b><br><br>My Casting:<br><br><b>Clay</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417179i/824861._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Maggie</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379790983i/544228._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“She glanced over her shoulder as she made her way into the restaurant, as though to make sure I was still waiting for her. <br><i>You crazy girl, don’t you know I’d wait for you forever?”</i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417179i/824862._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Enjoy!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1088632332630793096" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_572154143" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/572154143" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/572154143?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own">pb-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer572154143" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1335176844576569042"><b>ABSOLUTE FREAKING PERFECTION!</b><br/><br/>This book gave me everything that I wanted! It picks up the story several months after the ending of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_' title='Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters' rel='nofollow noopener'>Find You in the Dark</a>, and we get both Clay and Maggie’s POVs as they struggle to pick up the pieces of their lives and move on after the shattering events of the last book. <br/><br/>Clay and Maggie are apart for the first part of the book. Both desperately trying to find a way to move on without each other. When a tragedy brings him home to Davidson, they are thrust back into </span>
  <span id="freeText1335176844576569042" style="display:none"><b>ABSOLUTE FREAKING PERFECTION!</b><br /><br />This book gave me everything that I wanted! It picks up the story several months after the ending of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_" title="Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">Find You in the Dark</a>, and we get both Clay and Maggie’s POVs as they struggle to pick up the pieces of their lives and move on after the shattering events of the last book. <br /><br />Clay and Maggie are apart for the first part of the book. Both desperately trying to find a way to move on without each other. When a tragedy brings him home to Davidson, they are thrust back into each other’s worlds, unable to stay away from each other. Their love for each other is still very much there, but they have a twisted and dysfunctional past, as well as very serious issues in the present. There are massive obstacles for them to overcome if they want to be together. <br /><br />But Maggie is absolutely committed to Clay.<br /><br /><i>“I still hung onto the hope that my broken knight would gallop back into my life and sweep me off my feet.”<br /><br />“My feelings hadn’t changed. And even though I didn’t trust him with my heart, it was his nonetheless.”</i><br /><br />And Clay is absolutely determined to be a better man – for Maggie and for himself.<br /><br /><i>“God, I loved her. She was the piece I had been missing for the last three months. She was everything I wanted in my life but was still unsure I deserved.”<br /><br />“You are everything good in my life. Even when I thought all I had was the darkness, you were there. And you gave me something to live for. I couldn’t let you go. No matter how hard I tried. I know now that’s because to lose you would be losing the very best part of myself.”</i><br /><br />This is a super emotional read. There are ups and downs, and you feel everything right alongside the characters. But it’s also incredibly realistic. There is no easy fix in this story. Even though Clay and Maggie love each other deeply, they have to work at being together, and trying to create a life together - Clay, in particular, has a lot of work to do. And I loved that their struggle was laid out for us in fantastic detail. It was emotionally raw and honest, but also sensitive and absolutely beautiful. <br /><br />These are the kind of characters that stay with you forever. They both have their vulnerabilities, but they are both incredibly strong, and I admire them so much for all that they go through, how they cope with it while it’s all happening, their honesty with each other, the decisions they make, and their devotion to each other without being totally stupid about it. They have both changed so much from the characters we met in the first book, and I love how they are both so willing to face the realities of their situation and fight hard for what they want. <br /><br /><i>“Ignoring things didn’t make them go away. It only made it harder to face them when they finally came around to beat the shit out of you.”</i><br /><br />Clay and Maggie’s story is absolutely incredible, and I have loved every minute of their journey. As a bonus, we get to follow Daniel and Rachel’s story, which fits alongside the main storyline brilliantly. And we get to see all four of these beloved characters in a sensational epilogue which closes off the story beautifully.<br /><br />I laughed, I cried, I squeed and I swooned. I totally and utterly loved it. 5 shining stars.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I can only say, with one hundred percent certainty that I love you. That I live and breathe for you. That I would lay down my life a million times over for you. And no matter what happens tomorrow, next week, next year, my heart will always be yours.”</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="1335176844576569042" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('DwHeKILI2vDXGcXZCQtl/BoO602wuIXAwjWAn3liuRBnYpiCLWa7artZX4A6V4tumD6StXAwdZezcO6r3Tdzjw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('eykjyzdau98oUoD7foqfursau3v/LiI5OiZHy+uNCzUTSmVhmPTaRUQSGqJN1nEoOSrCgz+m0m5LYyn/T9jBqg==')})
  }
//]]>
